Current Commentary

The Silver Question and the World Economic Conference 32

Arise from the Internal and External Conflicts of Interest Among Capitalist Powers. International Conferences are becoming increasingly frequent as internal and external conflicts of interest among capitalist powers become increasingly acute. In peaceful times, one lives quietly behind closed doors. When disaster strikes, one cannot help but gather neighbors to plan a response. The same is true of the international situation. Therefore, international conferences with a myriad of titles are a clear indication of the helplessness of the statesmen of the great powers. The fact that these conferences are frequent but yield little results clearly shows that although those in power are doing their utmost to make a last stand, they may ultimately be unable to stem the tide.

Although there are many international conferences, they can be broadly divided into two types: universal and regional. The former, such as the past silver conference and disarmament conference, center on the major powers and treat the smaller countries as mere accessories. The latter, such as the Lausanne Conference and the Ottawa Conference, involve either a segment of the major powers or are limited to a certain imperial power and its colonies. From a broader perspective, universal international conferences, other than allowing certain celebrities to utter lofty but impractical proposals and make empty, self-deceiving declarations, are essentially useless. On the other hand, regional conferences are often able to formulate more practical plans and bring about temporary, minor changes in the economic sphere. For example, as a result of the Lausanne Conference, Britain, France, Germany, and Italy unanimously advocated to the United States to cancel war debts. As a result of the Ottawa Conference, the United States reduced its export trade by 100 million gold yuan. All these instances illustrate the plight of the capitalist powers, which are outwardly strong but inwardly weak, and are struggling to make ends meet in the face of the deepening global panic. The so-called rescue measures are merely aimed at benefiting one's neighbors and temporarily prolonging one's own survival, but the increasing conflicts and contradictions within global capitalism are accelerating its demise. Seeking a balanced solution in a universal international conference is almost impossible given the current state of affairs.

Following the regional Lausanne Conference and Ottawa Conference, preparations are now underway for a universal World Economic Conference. Britain, having solidified the European powers' front against the United States at the Lausanne Conference and demonstrated the unity of the British Empire and its threat to the United States at the Ottawa Conference, has gradually regained its former position of rivaling the United States. By meeting with the United States from this position at an international conference, it may be hoped that the United States will slightly change its past domineering attitude and accept the European nations' demands for the cancellation of war debts. Therefore, in the eyes of European nations, the war debt issue is originally the main agenda of the World Economic Conference. As a result, the so-called World Economic Conference is essentially nothing more than a great power's debt reliance conference.

US President Hoover, having seen through this hidden agenda, initially declared that the war debt issue could not be discussed. Subsequently, in his campaign speeches and recent statements, he proposed the silver issue as the main agenda of the World Economic Conference. In this regard, we must recognize that the so-called World Economic Conference cannot escape the legacy of past universal international conferences and will ultimately dissolve without results. The status of the silver issue in this conference is merely a tool for Hoover to counter the European powers' focus on war debts. It is almost the same as the Japanese's intention to raise the issue of racial equality at the Washington Conference. Since the speaker's real intention is not wine, its futility is already evident.

However, the silver issue must be discussed at least once in the upcoming World Economic Conference because its history and its position in public opinion make it an unavoidable fact. The solution to the silver issue comes down to two options: limiting production or increasing its usage. Increasing its usage is mainly focused on restoring silver coinage. On this point, there is already a wonderful argument in American public opinion: "If silver is cheap, must we use silver for coinage? If cotton is cheap, must we also use cotton for coinage?" Since the authority of the theory of controlled currency has long surpassed the theory of international bimetallism after European countries abandoned the gold standard, the restoration of silver coinage has become a relic of the past. The discussion will undoubtedly center on limiting production.

Limiting production will again lead to conflict. The world's largest silver-producing countries, the United States and Mexico, will undoubtedly attribute the drastic decline in silver prices to India's sale of its silver reserves, while Britain, the protector of India, will certainly deny this and advocate for restrictions on silver mine production. Since both sides have their own reasons, it is doubtful whether a conciliatory solution can be found. Recalling the failure of the past British-Dutch rubber production restriction agreement, and considering that the production of silver is even more widespread than that of rubber, one can see that a restrictive plan will be difficult to formulate.

The above is merely to illustrate the difficulty of resolving the silver issue and to prevent the people of our country from entertaining unnecessary illusions. As for the impact of raising silver prices on our country's economy, it is beyond the scope of this article.

Five Major Powers to Convene Meeting to Discuss German Demands 65

British Prime Minister and French Premier to Attend Personally

National News Agency, Geneva, 25th - Talks regarding Germany's demand for military equality have finally materialized into a concrete plan. A meeting will be held by the five major powers to discuss this matter, tentatively scheduled for December 2nd. It is reported that this plan was agreed upon during separate meetings today between German Foreign Minister Neurath, US representative Davis, and British Foreign Secretary Simon. Afterwards, Davis and Simon departed for Paris. Simon will return to London after meeting with Herriot, while Neurath will return to his country on Saturday. According to reliable sources, British Prime Minister MacDonald and French Premier Herriot will personally attend the five major power conference.

National News Agency, Paris, 25th - It is confirmed today that French Premier Herriot will go to Geneva on Thursday, staying for several days. Political circles believe this action indirectly confirms the informal agreement of the five major powers to discuss Germany's demand for military equality.

The Situation After the US Reply Rejecting Debt Moratorium is Published 66

Has Caused Upheaval in Political Circles and Sparked Disputes Between Britain and France

National News Agency, Paris, 25th - A major upheaval has occurred in political circles here. The reason is that the United States is unwilling to suspend or postpone war debt payments. Britain then contacted France, requesting that France continue to repay its debts. However, French Premier Herriot indicated unwillingness to discuss this matter, as the French parliament would certainly not approve debt payments under the current circumstances. However, Britain, in view of France's unwillingness to repay war debts, consulted with the United States, stating that Britain was willing to deduct France's debt to Britain from Britain's debt to the United States and repay the remaining amount. Therefore, under this plan, Britain would only need to pay the United States $54 million. French public opinion is extremely indignant about this, considering it an attempt to shift the blame onto France and undermine the united European front. The French government has not yet made a formal statement on this matter, but it has acknowledged its significance.

US Reply: Cannot Abandon Original Agreement 67

Reuters, London, 25th - President Hoover's reply to the British government's request for a moratorium on the £28 million debt due on December 15th was released today. The main points of the reply are as follows: In such an important matter, there must be no opportunity for misunderstanding or for the two countries to fail to reach a satisfactory solution. Congress has the final decision-making power. Reparations are a purely European issue that has nothing to do with the United States. The British dispatch of November 10th should not imply that the Lausanne reparations issue was resolved because of reliance on the US government. The US is deeply aware of the impact of the cessation of reparations on creditor nations. It also recognizes that global economic depression has increased the weight of debt. However, economic depression has also increased the burden on the American people, and the impact of modifying the war debt agreement on American taxpayers cannot be ignored. A mechanism similar to the former US World War Debt Committee should be established to investigate the conflicting elements in the global situation. Hoover did not state that the original agreement must be fully maintained with the November payment. This action is more important than any current argument for suspension. With this payment, the prospect of a satisfactory resolution to the entire issue will be greatly increased.

Havas, London, 25th - The US Secretary of State's reply to the British note of November 10th regarding the war debt issue has been delivered to the British government. The content of the reply is roughly as follows: [Your Excellency's note of November 10th, putting forward suggestions and explaining the seriousness of the situation, is clearly understood by me in its importance. Your government states that since there is an agreement between the two countries on the war debt issue, there is a need for modification. This alone is enough to cause deep concern. In such an important situation, the various points listed in Your Excellency's note should not be overlooked, so as to avoid misunderstandings or to ensure that a conclusion satisfactory to both governments and peoples can be reached. With this in mind, I would like to briefly explain to Your Excellency how my government intends to add conditions and restrictions to the modification of this issue. According to my country, the reorganization, reduction and modification of all debts is not only entirely within the power of Parliament, but judging from past facts, the organization handling such matters is also organized by Parliament itself. For example, the Foreign Debt Committee during the Great War is an example. The committee, when necessary, may order investigations and make recommendations to Parliament on the actions it deems appropriate. Its recommendations are submitted to Parliament for review, and the right to decide is exercised by Parliament, which relies on the intermediary of the mechanism to express its actions. Your government should know that Your Excellency's general modification proposal is far broader than the methods ever considered and proposed by President Hoover and the US government. Even if Your Excellency's note is only a suggestion, it is difficult for my country's parliament to endorse it.] The US reply specifically stated, [No one can say that the solution to the German reparations issue is due to some promise made by the United States.] The US reply continued, [The countries owed by your country for reparations have taken measures in Lausanne to resolve them, and the countries have therefore given up this income, but the world panic is constantly increasing the burden, and the stagnation of international industries is also enough to increase the difficulty of trade. I have never forgotten these two points. It must be understood that the burden added to the American people by this phenomenon of decline is also very heavy.] The conclusion of the US reply is extremely clear, roughly stating, [There is nothing in Your Excellency's note to make the US Congress abandon the principles it has adhered to in the past. Therefore, the US President believes that if we want to re-examine the current financial situation, we must create a mechanism to study this issue separately for the relevant countries. The US President is prepared to request Congress to create such a mechanism to study the entirety of this issue.] The reply also stated that regarding the British request to suspend the debt due on December 15th, the US administrative agency cannot recognize it without the permission of Congress. Finally, it stated [The US government and people believe that the payment due on December 15th should be paid as scheduled in order to respect the original agreement. The US government and people attach great importance to this level, so the reasons for advocating suspension have failed to convince them. If this agreement can be implemented, it will greatly facilitate satisfactory consideration of this issue.]

Havas, Paris, 25th - Although the US Secretary of State's reply to France regarding the war debt issue is more detailed than the reply to Britain, the views expressed and the reasons given are exactly the same.

Havas, Brussels, 26th - US Secretary of State Stimson's reply to Belgium regarding the request to suspend war debt payments was released here at 12:15 PM today. Its content is the same as the reply to France.

Britain and France Greatly Disappointed, French Public Opinion Particularly Agitated 68

Havas, Paris, 25th - The US President's rejection of the request for a moratorium on war debts has greatly disappointed political circles here. The parliamentary side believes that the reasons put forward by European countries are worthy of consideration. A Havas reporter sought opinions from members of various parties in the Chamber of Deputies, which were generally similar. The Vice-President of the Chamber of Deputies, a member of the Radical Socialist Party, said that when the Chamber of Deputies passed the Young Plan, it had made reservations, that is, France's payments to the US should be guaranteed by Germany's payment of reparations. The left-wing Republican Democratic Union member, De Monzie, said that France abandoned its claims against Germany because of Hoover's request. The left-wing Independent Party member, Ayre, said that the psychology of the Americans is increasingly incomprehensible. During the European war, the United States worked hard with European countries on the battlefield. France sacrificed the flesh and blood of its people, while the United States only supplied us with its goods. As for money, not a single cent was transported to Europe. American people have completely forgotten this fact. Ayre was quite sad when he spoke. Socialist Party member Vallon said that Hoover had relieved Germany of its burden, so that France was unable to repay its debts. Radical Party leader and chairman of the Chamber of Deputies Foreign Affairs Committee, Albert, was quite silent due to war affairs, but also said that no one believes that the payment due on December 15th will be repaid. From this, it can be seen that all the deputies believe that the US view is unfair, but everyone hopes that negotiations can still achieve a fair solution. Generally, people also believe that the difficulties experienced by the United States are also increasing day by day. Its refusal of the demands of European countries may also have unavoidable difficulties. However, if the spiritual and material capabilities of European countries are ignored, the difficulties of the United States itself and the decline of the world will be in even more serious danger.

It is my humble opinion that paying the amount due this time can greatly increase the hope of a satisfactory resolution to the entire issue. Reuters, London, 26th - President Hoover's reply did not ease concerns in London, as the reply did not request detailed facts on the promised suspension of the British debt in December, but only expressed disregard for agreeing to the suspension. Amid the current chaotic exchange market, newspapers disagree on whether Britain has a way to repay its debt. Britain to Draft Reply Swiftly 69

Reuters, London, 25th - The British government will send out a reply to the US President as soon as possible after a cabinet meeting on Monday. According to informed sources in London, the reasons given by Treasury experts for postponing debt payments will be extremely powerful, which can persuade US congressmen who currently oppose suspension to support President Hoover's suggestion. If it is proven that paying in cash immediately due to currency depreciation and other reasons will cause a crisis, it may not be impossible to make concessions. Today, Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain spoke in Birmingham, referring to the Lausanne Conference, saying that everyone hoped that there would be no need to reopen the issue of the Allied powers repaying war debts after that, but we never expected that we would have to pay debts, the amount of which is equivalent to an increase of one shilling per pound in income tax, and at the same time we have no income from debtor countries. This kind of situation cannot be tolerated from the perspective of justice or from the perspective of maintaining British industrial prosperity. British Prime Minister MacDonald also made remarks on the war debt issue in Leith today, saying that people with good intentions who understand the unfortunate current situation of the world, if they truly work together, if both sides put themselves in each other's shoes, he does not believe that a solution cannot be found to deal with the payment due on December 15th, to study the future of the payment, and to conclude a new agreement. The debts Britain lent to the Allied powers are almost equal to the debts Britain owes the United States. Britain has reduced what people owe it by 60%, and the amount Britain pays to the United States is 200 million pounds more than what Britain receives from Europe. Britain has not asked to cancel or reduce, but only requested to postpone the payment period. The discussion of debts between the two countries has now caused ill feelings between the two countries.

Important News

Su Bingwen Refuses Japanese Pleas for Peace 76

The Japanese military entrusted the Russian consulate to convey a request for a meeting, but Su did not reply. Japanese representatives find themselves in a dilemma. 丨The Su and Zhang armies construct solid defensive positions to await the enemy.丨丨The Japanese army plans to use Mongolian cavalry for a flanking attack.丨 According to a Hailar dispatch, after Su Bingwen detained eight hundred and forty Japanese residents in the Manchouli and Hailar areas, the Japanese, in an attempt to rescue their nationals, used humble words and generous gifts to plead for peace with Su, hoping to trick their nationals out and then advance towards the Xing'an Mountains. The Japanese side believes this cunning plan is foolproof. However, Su Bingwen has been meticulously planning for a year and, with his superior talent and knowledge, saw through this deceptive tactic long ago. He knew his strength was insufficient and feared he could not hold out for long, so he used the Japanese plea for peace to buffer the war. Although written messages are constantly exchanged, in reality, he is still preparing. The Japanese previously sent Xie Ke to Hulunbuir to persuade Su to surrender to the puppet state, but to no avail. This spring, Xie was captured by the Japanese in Dalian while returning to Beiping via Vladivostok. He was imprisoned in Harbin for several months and released a few days before the Manchouli Incident. He was forced to serve the puppet state in Heilongjiang, but he had long harbored ambitions of revenge. Unable to find an opportunity, he immediately refused when asked to be the representative to persuade Su, and became Su's chief of staff, assisting Zhang Dianjiu in planning the military operations in the front lines. The Japanese, seeing that the puppet representative was unreliable, had no choice but to assign Colonel Komatsubara, the chief of the Harbin Special Service Agency under the Kwantung Army, as the head of the negotiation committee, to invite Su to a meeting at Masievka on the Soviet-Russian border. They first entrusted Strotsky, the Russian consul in Harbin, to negotiate with Trunov, the Russian consul in Manchouli, to persuade Su to meet on November 12. On that day, Komatsubara, accompanied by Major Fuzaki of the Harbin Special Service Agency, Lieutenant Colonel Hashimoto of the Kwantung Army Staff, Captain Okada, Captain Miyazaki, translator Endo, Wang Jizhong, the head of the Armaments Section of the puppet state's Ministry of Military Affairs, and Shao Lin, a supervisor of the Chinese Eastern Railway, a group of fifteen people, traveled from Harbin to Qiqihar. On the morning of the 13th at 6:25 AM, they boarded two planes and flew to the Russian border, landing at Dauri. The Soviet Russians were quite wary of Japanese aircraft entering their territory, fearing they would scout out border secrets. Therefore, the Harbin consulate had informed the Japanese beforehand that aircraft entering the border should not circle in the air and should land at the designated location. In the afternoon of the 13th, when the Japanese planes arrived at Dauri, the Soviet Russian border guards suddenly held a large-scale military parade in Dauri, showcasing their military might and implying that they were well-equipped and highly trained. After Komatsubara and others disembarked, they were transported to Masievka on the border by a special Russian train, using a third-class carriage. Armed soldiers were stationed before and after the carriage, ostensibly for protection, but the Japanese were not allowed to carry weapons after getting off the train, nor were they allowed to take walks outside the station. In reality, it was the same as monitoring all their external communications. Although it appeared to be freedom, the Russians had secretly set up radio receivers nearby to intercept any messages. The Japanese experienced this situation and dared not express any complaints. When Komatsubara and others flew over Hailar, they dropped documents from the plane requesting that Su Bingwen send representatives or personally go to Masievka for a meeting. After arriving at Masievka, they sent a telegram to Manchouli requesting the dispatch of representatives, but Su did not reply. These Japanese have fallen into a dilemma. The Kwantung Army Headquarters could not help but become annoyed. On the one hand, they ordered Komatsubara to study countermeasures and promote negotiations, while on the other hand, they vigorously transported Japanese troops stationed in southern Manchuria to concentrate in the Ang'angxi area to create a show of support. However, Su Bingwen had already made full military arrangements. He recently informed the Russian consul in Manchouli that he refused to send representatives for negotiations. The Russian consul telegraphed its Foreign Affairs Committee, which relayed it to the Japanese. Although the Japanese knew that negotiations were hopeless, they were still trying hard to collect information on people related to Su Bingwen, persuading Su to release the nationals and surrender to the puppet state. Ji Xiang, the former chairman of the Heilongjiang puppet Security Maintenance Association, who was acquainted with Su, was also used by the Japanese to send telegrams to persuade him. Currently, the Su and Zhang armies, after a fierce battle with the Japanese army at Qianhou Kuler on November 10, Wu Delin's brigade rushed to the front lines from Manchouli to reinforce.

They are now constructing a solid defensive position at Gefenshan, seven miles from Houkuler. The troops are concentrated at Nianzishan, Zhalantun, Zhujiakan. Gefenshan is eighteen miles from Zhujiakan, Nianzishan is sixty miles from Zhujiakan, and Zhalantun is sixty miles from Nianzishan. The troop deployment is extremely secret, and all have built solid trenches. The Japanese army and the puppet cavalry brigade are guarding the area around Hulhuyu and Yaokuler, with the two sides' positions very close. However, the Japanese army must wait for its Sixth Division to arrive before launching an offensive. Recently, it was heard that someone offered a plan to Wu..., ordering the use of Mongolian cavalry to flank Hailar from the Solon grasslands, while the Japanese army attacked from the front along the railway. The Japanese side believes that this plan is worth adopting, so in the future, they may use Zhang Hai's army to attack nearby from the grasslands. The Japanese military plan this spring originally intended to station a brigade or so in the Xing'an Mountains to control the area and prevent Su Bingwen from acting. However, their forces were repeatedly restrained by Ma Zhanshan's and Ding Li's armies, so they were unable to send troops forward. Therefore, recently, both the Japanese government and the public have blamed the Kwantung Army Headquarters for failing to implement this plan. (November 18)

Soviet Commemoration Under Japanese Surveillance 77

An expanded celebration is held, and the director's speech contains veiled references. Russia does not treat the puppet diplomats with courtesy. The eight stations of the Chinese Eastern Railway continue to operate factories, and the Japanese can do nothing about it.

Changchun Dispatch: This year's anniversary of the Soviet October Revolution coincided with the fifteenth week after the establishment of the state. The celebration was held simultaneously at home and abroad on the designated day of November 7th. The Red Russians residing in the Northeast were all summoned by the Consul-General in Harbin and held the event in Harbin. Amidst the dense Japanese presence, the Russian Consul in Harbin, together with Kuzmichov, the Deputy Director of the Chinese Eastern Railway, and Rudyi, the Director of the Railway Bureau, had prepared for the expanded celebration one month in advance. All arrangements were dozens of times more detailed than previous years. All Soviet shops and agencies were decorated with lanterns and flags, and the electric lights were brilliant at night, extremely magnificent. Between the roofs of the Chinese Eastern Railway Bureau and the clubhouse, there were colorful paintings depicting the scene of the Soviet May Day military parade, with tanks, airplanes, artillery, and other powerful weapons. Viewed under the lights at night, they appeared even more imposing. All of this was unprecedented. But they should not think that we are standing by with our hands in our pockets, doing nothing. The Red Army is guarding the Soviet border and can be dispatched at any time. We can also help at any time." The meaning of the words was suggestive, and not empty words. On that day, the puppet police agencies, under Japanese control, took strict precautions. Each street was specially closed early, prohibiting people from passing through. However, the Soviet personnel had no other actions except for celebration and joy. The Soviet attitude towards the Japanese side is really unpredictable. The high-sounding treaty of non-aggression between Japan, Manchuria, and the Soviet Union is neither explicitly endorsed by the Soviet Union, nor is it denied. Although the puppet state's consul Huang Hongchi, stationed in Heihe, is allowed to reside there, he is not treated as a diplomat, and he is not allowed to participate in any international ceremonies. Our consul Lin Shi'en, stationed in Heihe, is still under Russian protection. Japanese propaganda that the Soviet Union has expelled him and returned him to his country is inaccurate. When the Chinese in Heihe saw that the puppet state had actually sent a consul, they were outraged and distributed leaflets demanding that the Soviet Union expel him. As for the matter of the Jiangyun Office of the puppet state forcibly taking back the pier at the eight stations of the Chinese Eastern Railway in Harbin, the negotiations have not yet been resolved. The Chinese Eastern Railway is still setting up a field office in the vicinity of the old pier and still operating its office. The puppet state has negotiated many times and cannot do anything about it. This also proves that the Soviet Union's handling of the puppet state is purely out of cunning tactics, making it difficult for the Japanese behind the scenes to deal with. (November 9)

The Anglo-Russian Trade Agreement Problem - London Correspondence by Xin Sheng

The Conservative Party advocates abolition.

Samuel criticizes it.

丨The machinery industry is feared to suffer a major blow.丨 At a time when the international status of Soviet Russia is increasing day by day and diplomatic relations are progressing, the British government suddenly took the step of abolishing the Anglo-Russian trade agreement, and there had been no conflict between the two countries beforehand that would have changed each other's feelings. We suddenly heard on the 19th of this month that the British government had changed its policy towards Russia and decided to abolish the trade agreement after six months. The matter is indeed worthy of surprise. We cannot know the motive behind the British government's attitude. The government has not put forward any major reasons for this matter, so onlookers mostly regard it as impossible. European public opinion also has many speculations. But judging from the words of Thomas to the House of Commons, the true intention is not difficult to guess. Since the establishment of the National Cabinet, the British political power has been transferred to the hands of the Conservative Party. Recently, since Samuel, Snowden, and others withdrew, the National Cabinet has become a mere formality. In fact, it has become a Conservative government of one color. The fundamental policy of the Conservative Party is only to safeguard the interests of the special class. It does not care much about the prosperity and decline of industry, the prosperity and decline of trade, the interests of industrialists, or the number of unemployed people. Their concept of Soviet Russia is deeply dominated by traditional thinking. Therefore, it is not surprising that the Conservative Party's relationship with Russia will fundamentally change after it comes to power. The industrial sector, for the sake of its own interests, will certainly oppose it, especially the machinery manufacturing industry. At present, the leaders of the British industrial sector are strongly opposing the government's policy towards Russia. The Samuel faction of the Liberal Party is especially criticizing it. Samuel said that the government's move is actually giving a new blow to the empire's foreign trade. As a result, unemployment will increase and the crisis will become more serious. The Labour Party's opposition is needless to say. But the Conservative government turns a blind eye to this and does not care. Since the conclusion of the Anglo-Russian trade agreement, the number of British exports to Russia has increased greatly. In 1929, British exports to Russia were only 3.7 million pounds, but by 1931, it had increased to 7.1 million pounds (tea exports were not included). This year it continued to increase, with the increase in the first half of the year reaching 3.2 million pounds. Therefore, according to this trend, British exports to Russia are on the rise. Unexpectedly, the Conservative government did not pay attention to this and resolutely wanted to sever ties with Russia. It is no wonder that Samuel regarded it as a new blow. However, this is only in general. If we go on to analyze the individual sectors of British industry, the impact of this policy towards Russia is even more visible. In fact, the export of British machinery to Europe is almost entirely limited to Soviet Russia. In 1931, the export of British machine tools to Soviet Russia accounted for 75% of the total exports. Mining machinery imported into Soviet Russia accounted for 47% of the total exports. Turbines imported into Soviet Russia accounted for 78% of the total exports. Compressors accounted for 54%. It is difficult to enumerate other examples. Therefore, the market for Lancashire machinery manufacturing is mainly in Soviet Russia. Lloyd's Trade Report stated that 80% of British machinery exports must be sold to Soviet Russia, which is a fact. Therefore, the fundamental change in British policy towards Russia will undoubtedly be a blow to the British machinery manufacturing industry first. The Conservative Party has never taken into account the future of the industrial sector and has put the interests of the special class first. It is feared that it will increase the British crisis and become thorny. The Manchester Weekly Newspaper said that the British government's move was made lightly and did not take into account the interests of foreign trade. It is deeply aware of this. (October 21)

The Legislative Yuan Passes

Organizational Regulations of the Bureau of Commodity Inspection 78

The Legislative Yuan held its 214th meeting on the morning of the 26th, and revised and passed the fifteen articles of the Organizational Regulations of the Bureau of Commodity Inspection, which are recorded as follows: (Organizational Regulations of the Bureau of Commodity Inspection of the Ministry of Industry). Article 1: The Bureau of Commodity Inspection shall be established by the Ministry of Industry upon approval by the Executive Yuan in the main commercial ports for foreign trade to implement inspection affairs in accordance with the Commodity Inspection Law. Article 2: The Bureau of Commodity Inspection shall have an Administrative Office and an Inspection Office. Article 3: The Administrative Office shall be in charge of documents, accounting, general affairs, statistics, editing, and matters not belonging to the Inspection Office. Article 4: The Inspection Office may be divided into groups to be in charge of the technical matters of commodity inspection. Article 5: When there is a situation as stipulated in the proviso of Article 3 of the Commodity Inspection Law, after the Bureau of Commodity Inspection submits it to the Ministry of Industry for submission to the Executive Yuan for approval, an Inspection Branch may be established. Article 6: The Bureau of Commodity Inspection shall have one Director, who shall, under the order of the Ministry of Industry, comprehensively manage the affairs of the entire Bureau and supervise the staff. Article 7: The Bureau of Commodity Inspection shall have two Office Directors, who shall, under the order of the Director, manage the affairs of each Office. Article 8: The Bureau of Commodity Inspection shall have ten to twenty Clerks, who shall, under the order of their superiors, be responsible for their duties. Article 9: The Bureau of Commodity Inspection shall have two to ten Technicians, four to fourteen Assistant Technicians, and seven to twenty Technical Assistants, who shall handle technical affairs under the order of their superiors. Article 10: The Inspection Branch shall have one Director, who shall concurrently be a Technician, and who shall, under the order of the Director of the Bureau, manage all affairs of the Branch. Article 11: The Inspection Branch shall have one Technician, one to two Assistant Technicians, one to three Technical Assistants, and two to four Clerks, who shall, under the order of their superiors, be responsible for their respective duties. Article 12: The number of Technicians, Assistant Technicians, Technical Assistants, and Clerks shall be separately drafted by the Directors of each Bureau according to the complexity of the affairs and submitted to the Ministry of Industry for approval. Article 13: The Director of the Bureau of Commodity Inspection shall be Recommended Appointment or Simplified Appointment, the Office Director and Technician shall be Recommended Appointment, and the Assistant Technician, Technical Assistant, and Clerk shall be Appointed Appointment. Article 14: The Bureau of Commodity Inspection may employ Employees and may also accept Trainees. Article 15: This Regulation shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Jilin Province Volunteer Army Sheds Blood to Resist Japan 79

Fu Dianchen and Luo Mingxing Repeatedly Defeat the Stubborn Enemy. The Japanese Plan to Eliminate the Volunteer Army Fails. The Brave Men on the Banks of the Songhua River Will Have Great Achievements. Tianjin Dispatch: According to a person from Changchun, since the autumn harvest in Guanwai has been completed, the green gauze curtains have fallen, and there is an endless view, which has caused the armed people who are resisting Japan and suppressing the rebels to lose their reliance. The Japanese Kwantung Army authorities have decided to implement a plan to eliminate our volunteer army in stages. The first phase that has been implemented is the encirclement and suppression of Tang Juwu and other troops in Liaodong (Japanese forces: one division and 50 aircraft). According to Japanese propaganda, this first phase of the plan has been completed. In fact, in order to avoid air raids and unnecessary sacrifices, Tang's army voluntarily abandoned Tonghua and other seven or eight counties and retreated to the deep mountains and ridges in the Mengjiang area, waiting for an opportunity to rise again. It can be said that they are temporarily lying low, but they have not yet been scattered. The second phase of the plan is to encircle and suppress the volunteer armies in the triangular area south of the Jichang Road, west of the Ji-Hai and Shen-Hai Roads, and east of the Mantetsu Railway, with the same force used in the first phase, about 15,000 men. The most powerful volunteer army in this triangular area is the Northeast National Salvation Army led by Fu Dianchen (Commander of the 7th Independent Detachment), with a total of about 30,000 men. For the past year, they have occupied Panshi, Shuangyang, and other counties, as well as key locations along the Ji-Hai Railway, repeatedly defeating the stubborn enemy. The Ji-Hai Railway has been blocked for a long time, which is the achievement of Fu Dianchen and other troops. Shuangyang County was once captured by them in the summer of this year. No less than 3,000 puppet soldiers, police, and Japanese soldiers were killed or disarmed. Fu enjoys a high reputation in the southern Jilin area. His military discipline is strict, and the local people have a good impression of him and are willing to help him. Therefore, the Japanese traitors are deeply jealous of him. They often tempt him with fame and fortune, but he has always been sternly rejected by Fu. Before the Japanese army launched the offensive, they repeatedly sent people to persuade Fu to surrender to the puppet state and promised him high positions. Fu was furious when he heard this and immediately detained and imprisoned the envoys to express his determination to resist the enemy to the death. Seeing that their plan had failed, the Japanese army sent Ogawa, Fujii, and other troops, together with Zhang Haipeng and other rebel troops, to launch a fierce attack with their aircraft, artillery, tanks, and other powerful weapons from the 11th of this month. At that time, it was snowing heavily and the weather was extremely cold. Fu Dianchen and other commanders led their troops, braving the cold and freezing, and bravely resisted the enemy's artillery fire. The enemy's artillery fire was extremely fierce, and the aircraft bombing was particularly cruel. The volunteer army lacked ammunition and felt extremely difficult, resulting in heavy casualties and a tragic sight. However, because the bloodstains of the dead were reflected in the minds of the living, morale was high and the military spirit was strengthened. Therefore, they were able to follow each other and fight bloody hand-to-hand combat. Everyone raised their arms and shouted, and the sounds of killing shook the sky. Even the fierce and stubborn enemy was frightened and intimidated. Fu, the commander, and other cadres and officers, in order to change the strategy, ordered their troops to withdraw from the railway line from Yantongshan Chalukouhe (7th Detachment Headquarters). About 4,000 men of the troops retreating from Yantongshan suddenly appeared near Huadian a few days later. Fearing that they would respond to Wang Delin's troops and attack the Jidun Railway, the Japanese side urgently increased troops from Jilin and Changchun to guard. As for those retreating from Chalukouhe, about 10,000 men, they scattered into several groups and marched towards Shaoguotun, Nianzigou, Dahuangdi, Fangniugou, Xinminbao (the above places are west of Ji-Hai and south of Ji-Chang). Changchun enemy rebels specially dispatched troops to block them, and there have been several fierce battles. Detailed situation is currently unknown, but the Japanese counter-propaganda is not credible. In addition, the volunteer armies in various places north of Ji-Chang Road, seeing that the friendly troops south of Ji-Chang Road were being besieged by the enemy, were outraged and eager to try to attack the enemy's back to support the friendly troops in the fierce battle. The first to launch the attack was the National Salvation Army 19th Independent Detachment led by Luo Mingxing. On the evening of the 17th, Luo personally led 3,000 cadres to suddenly attack Yingchengzi Station on the Ji-Chang Road from [redacted]. After three hours of bloody battle, the puppet railway garrison and the public security team were defeated and fled. Luo's army occupied the station and swept away all the ticket offices, dormitories, and various facilities. At the same time, another unit severely demolished a railway bridge between Yingchengzi and Xiajiutai, and two railway bridges between Xiajiutai and Yinmahe, and cut down more than a dozen electric poles and wires to block the Japanese army's traffic. Another unit attacked the street market in Xiajiutai. The Japanese residents living in the town scrambled to escape. A Japanese armored train from Changchun to support derailed and overturned two cars, killing and injuring more than 30 people due to the destruction of bridges on the way. Telegraph and telephone communications between Jilin and Changchun were completely cut off, and passenger and freight trains were also suspended. The puppet government was extremely shocked when it heard the news. It was not until dawn on the 18th that Luo's army voluntarily retreated, and the Japanese rebels were able to settle their frightened souls. At present, the Jilin and Changchun areas are indeed shrouded in an atmosphere of terror and tension. It is also heard that the brave men on the banks of the Songhua River, hating the Japanese rebels' brutality, are also eager to try. Soon there may be an even more magnificent and amazing performance. (November 24)

Guangzhou Dispatch: Since Yu Hanmou, the commander of the 1st Army of Guangdong, returned to southern Jiangxi to take up defense duties, he has been carrying out the second phase of the suppression of communist bandits. He Jian Requests Appropriations

Dredging Dongting Lake with American Wheat Funds 81

Utilizing American Wheat Loans to Dredge Dongting Lake

Establishing a Special Engineering Bureau

Changsha Communication: The central government has borrowed 450,000 tons of American wheat in two installments, valued at approximately 12 million US dollars, for the purpose of dredging rivers and undertaking water conservancy projects. The plan only established four engineering bureaus: Jianghan, Jiangxi, Jianghuai, and Jiangyun, without considering Dongting Lake, the largest water conservancy project in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. He Jian, Chairman of Hunan Province, believes that the allocation is not fair and the project is unbalanced. He specifically sent Wang Huixian, the Chief of the Dongting Lake Water Conservancy Survey Team, as a representative to Nanjing to negotiate, requesting that a portion of Dongting Lake be separately established as a special bureau to share the American wheat loans for dredging, in order to develop water conservancy in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. Representative Wang is scheduled to carry He Jian's petition to Nanjing on the 24th. The original text is recorded as follows: [Since the breaching of the Ouchi embankment in Hunan, Dongting Lake has been largely silted up. The amount of water from the upper reaches of the Yangtze River flowing into Dongting Lake accounts for nearly two-thirds, while only one-third flows directly down the old channel to the Yangtze River. With the large flow into Dongting Lake, the silt from the Sichuan River flows backward more and more, leading to a smaller lake surface. Every time the water rises in spring and summer, flooding occurs everywhere. Not only do the counties along the lake suffer greatly, but the entire Yangtze River basin is also affected by upstream breaches. Traditionally, those who discuss water conservancy invariably advocate dredging rivers and lakes simultaneously as a fundamental prevention method. However, this project is extremely large and costly, and it cannot be undertaken by a local area alone. It must rely on the central water conservancy authorities to coordinate and consider comprehensively for it to be successful. Recently, the National Government organized the National Economic Commission, which, based on the foundations of the provincial labor relief bureaus established last year, separately merged and established four engineering bureaus: Jianghan, Jiangxi, Jianghuai, and Jiangyun, to engage in river dredging projects. The funding comes from the second American wheat loan. Whether the American wheat should be borrowed or not is another issue, which will not be discussed here. However, in terms of the matter itself, since the central government has borrowed heavily to undertake national water conservancy, neglecting Dongting Lake, the most important in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, the handling of the overall water conservancy administration is unbalanced, and the allocation of people's rights and obligations is not fair. Moreover, Hunan Province originally established a labor relief bureau last year, and the first American wheat loan has already been allocated as appropriate. Later, due to special circumstances, the relief was changed to loans. This is only a slight change in the relief procedure, and the fundamental issue of water management must not be ignored. If the central government believes that the Hunan Provincial Labor Relief Bureau was abolished midway, and therefore does not allow its inclusion in this permanent engineering plan, it would inevitably abandon the fundamental and arouse people's doubts. It is earnestly requested that a portion of Dongting Lake be designated as a special bureau, ensuring that the use of national debt borne by the people of the whole country is transparently fair, and that the water conservancy projects that most people expect will not be neglected. This would not only be the good fortune of Hunan Province alone.] (November 23rd)

Special Report

Zhangjia Promotes Mongolian Banners (Continued) by Li Jianzhang 82

Furthermore, regarding the Mongolian banners, the Mongols' belief in Buddhism has almost become second nature, with Lamaism as the state religion. The survival of the religion is truly related to the entire Mongolian nation. Looking north to Outer Mongolia, after the spread of communism, with a thunderous sound, they immediately opposed Lamaism, burning monasteries and killing believers. The cruelty of the methods can be said to have reached the extreme. For the sake of their own survival, the banners of Inner Mongolia have no choice but to lean towards the central government, relying on the central government as a backup to jointly defend against foreign insults in order to protect their religion and preserve their race. Moreover, from China's point of view, Mongolia is naturally a part of China. However, from the Mongolian's point of view, it can also be Mongolia for the Mongols. However, since the communist takeover of Outer Mongolia, in just a few years, the number of Russians in Kulun has increased to over 50,000, enjoying various privileges and accounting for more than a quarter of the city's population. In contrast, the number of Chinese from the mainland who traveled to Mongolia was about 30,000 ten years ago, but now there are only over 2,000. Moreover, these 2,000 or so Chinese are all those who have sworn allegiance to communism; otherwise, they are not allowed to reside there. The speed of Russian population migration is astonishing. As for Japan, since it designated Manchuria as a special interest zone, economic aggression, cultural aggression, and military aggression have all been advancing simultaneously. The number of Japanese immigrants to Manchuria has increased dramatically. If they invade further and penetrate Inner Mongolia, they will continue to dedicate to Inner Mongolia what they have dedicated to Manchuria. The gradual increase in the number of Japanese and the gradual decrease in the number of Mongolians is inevitable without consideration. Thus, religious suppression leads to the disappearance of the common faith of the Mongols. The shrinking of land leads to the shrinking of the Mongols' nomadic areas. Economic decline makes it difficult for the Mongols' material life to continue. From the Mongols' point of view, and from the perspective of the entire future of the Mongolian banners, it is truly necessary to welcome the central government to urgently send senior officials to promote civilization.

However, who can bear this heavy responsibility, not failing the mission from above and not being useless to border defense from below? The matter is of great importance and should be considered calmly and weighed from various angles. If the wrong person is used, even good policies may be harmful. Let's discuss the Chinese and Mongols separately.

If a senior official with a long-standing reputation in the central government is sent to Mongolia with a mission to proclaim the country's virtues and answer the people's expectations, but considering the officials in the capital, there is no such figure who has gained sufficient trust from the Mongols. For someone who has no deep relationship with the Mongols to rashly go to Mongolia to promote civilization to the stubborn Mongols, it would be truly difficult to achieve substantial results.

Since it is not appropriate for Chinese to promote civilization in Mongolian banners, then it should be sought among the Mongols. The Mongolian princes are the leaders of the Mongolian banners and are also supported by the Mongols. However, the leader of this league cannot gain the trust of the people of that league, and at the same time, the leader of that league cannot gain the trust of the people of this league. Moreover, opinions among the leagues and banners are quite deep, and disputes often arise. If the central government entrusts any leader of one league with the mission of promoting civilization, it will inevitably provoke opposition from other leagues. This will not only fail to unite them but will also promote their internal strife. It is clear that the leaders of the leagues and banners cannot bear the full mission of promoting civilization. Then who can bear this mission? The answer is only the Zhangjia Hutuktu.

The Zhangjia Hutuktu is the leader of the Yellow Sect in Inner Mongolia. The Yellow Sect is another name for Lamaism, which originated in the Northern Song Dynasty, in the mid-7th century BC. Sakyamuni founded Buddhism in India. During the Tang Dynasty, it entered Tibet. In the sixth year of Emperor Xuanzong of the Tang Dynasty, the monks Shantarakshita and Padmasambhava from Uddiyana in India arrived in Tibet and began to transmit the esoteric teachings, which was the beginning of Lamaism's introduction to Tibet. The so-called esoteric teachings are Lamaism. The Mongol troops entered Tibet and took Lamaism with them. Kublai Khan, the Yuan Emperor, promoted it and appointed the Tibetan Grand Lama to the Tibetan government, honoring him as the Imperial Preceptor and Dharma King, and rewarding him for spreading the teachings. At that time, the Eighth Living Buddha of the Zhangjia Hutuktu was still in his original residence in Tangke, Qinghai, Tibet. The Yuan Emperor also sent officials to Tibet to welcome him to Yanjing to compile Mongolian scriptures, promote the Yellow Sect, establish temples in Inner Mongolia, manage the seals of important places, and preach in Inner Mongolia. Later, he ordered the Zhangjia Hutuktu to manage all the monks in Inner Mongolia, receiving the golden seal and being named Imperial Preceptor, in charge of the Yellow Sect in Inner Mongolia. He also followed the special decree of the Yuan Emperor and sent him back to Tibet to advise the Dalai Lama, Panchen Lama, and Jebtsundamba Khutuktu to serve as Living Buddhas, dividing them into Front Tibet, Back Tibet, and Outer Mongolia, each as the head of the sect. This was the beginning of the four Living Buddhas jointly managing the Yellow Sect in the two Mongolias and the two Tibets. Thus, the Zhangjia Hutuktu added the two characters "narrate merit" and "add irrigation" to his title. Since then, the position of the Zhangjia Hutuktu has been particularly prominent among the four Living Buddhas, being close to the capital and assisting in many meritorious deeds. After the Yuan Dynasty fell, Emperor Chengzu of the Ming Dynasty established the capital in Yanjing. In the twelfth year of Yongle, he also sent envoys to welcome the Tenth Living Buddha of the Zhangjia Hutuktu to Yanjing, and specially named him the Grand National Master, changing his seal to an eighty-eight tael gold seal. After the Ming Dynasty was overthrown, in the early years of Emperor Shizu Shunzhi of the Qing Dynasty, he welcomed the Zhangjia Hutuktu to the capital again and ordered him to assist in military affairs. Later, because he persuaded Inner Mongolia and other places such as Erte and Qinghai to submit, he ordered him to control the Khutuktu, Hobilghan, Noyanhan, and Khenpo Pandita Lamas in Inner Mongolia, and to manage the Buddhas in Inner Mongolia and other places as the head of the Eight Great Chan Masters Khutuktu, in charge of the seals of the capital, Shengjing, Wutai Mountain in Shanxi, Rehe, and Dolon Nor, and to manage the Yellow Sect in Inner Mongolia. During the three hundred years of the Qing Dynasty, the pacification of the border largely depended on this. The contributions of the successive Zhangjia Hutuktu to the central government cannot be compared to those of the other three Living Buddhas. The so-called Mongolian banners today, apart from the six leagues and one hundred and eleven banners of Outer Mongolia, are all called Inner Mongolia and belong to the Zhangjia Hutuktu's preaching area. Therefore, the meaning of Inner Mongolia is not limited to the three provinces of Suiyuan, Rehe, and Chahar. All areas where Inner Mongolian people reside and believe in the Yellow Sect belong to it. In terms of its scope, it extends north to the Khorchin Right Front Banner, Khorchin Left Front Banner, and other banners in Heilongjiang, east to the Jerim League banners in Liaoning Province, and west to the Alxa and Ejina banners in Gansu and Xinjiang provinces, all under the jurisdiction of the Zhangjia Hutuktu. With someone with such authority to promote civilization in the Mongolian banners, it would be like a father teaching his son and a teacher instructing his younger brother. It is naturally reasonable to expect him to be competent and happy. However, while the right person has been found, the embassy still needs to be strengthened, and the embassy itself must have great power in order to achieve its due effectiveness. Otherwise, drawing cakes to satisfy hunger will not help, and a clever woman cannot cook without rice. For the present, the Embassy of Civilization should be given full power, and the scope of the organization should not be too narrow, so that it can employ more talents and send them to various parts of Inner Mongolia to spread national prestige and encourage them to sincerely submit. It should also investigate the actual situation as a basis for developing Tibet and reforming politics, and awaken their national consciousness and organize them so that they can serve as a fence for border defense. After a long period of persuasion, the feelings of both sides will be harmonious, like hands and feet to the brain, and they will share weal and woe. When the brain gives an order, the hands and feet will move. When the hands and feet encounter stimulation, they will report to the brain. With a hundred responses to a single call, they will be flexible and free. The entire Chinese nation will be molded successfully, border troubles will be permanently eliminated, and foreign insults will naturally cease. How can Zhangjia's promotion of civilization in the Mongolian banners this time be compared to an ordinary mission? Drafted on November 23, 1921, at the Military Commission.

Songjiang 83

The Agricultural Bank Provides Rice Pledge Loans: The autumn harvest this year is abundant, but the price of rice has fallen, and farmers have suffered considerable losses. Often, when plowing, they borrow fertilizer and rice when rice prices are high, and when they repay the borrowed rice with the current harvest, they almost have to double it. Now, for the sake of farmers, the Songjiang branch of the Agricultural Bank is setting up warehouses to mortgage rice. It has rented large houses and will open immediately. The mortgage method is to discount the market price by 30%, with a monthly interest rate of 1%.

Suzhou 85

Bizarre Kidnapping Case: Xu Ganqing, a member of the Wuxian Security Committee and a native of Dongshan, lives at No. 10 Jiayu Lane in Suzhou City. Yesterday (the 26th), Xu and Jin Qingxia, a woman from Shanghai, were getting married at the Tianhexiang Auditorium on Lindun Road. Jin lives at No. 10 Wangjiazui in Shanghai and has been in Suzhou for two days. Just as the wedding ceremony was about to begin yesterday, Jin Xizhi, the woman's father, and her uncle, Zhi Zhi, suddenly reported to the Public Security Third District that the woman had been kidnapped by Xu to Suzhou, and that the woman had also taken away valuable jewelry and a 20,000 yuan passbook. They requested that the matter be investigated. The district sent detectives to Xu's home in Jiayu Lane, arrested Xu and the woman, and took them to the district for transfer to the local court. The testimonies were extremely complex and are recorded as follows: Jin Qingxia testified that she was 31 years old, a native of Suzhou, and lived at No. 73 Wangjiazui in Shanghai. She came to Suzhou from Shanghai on the 24th of this month and stayed at the New Suzhou Hotel. She has known Xu Ganqing for two years. This time, she came to Suzhou with her father, Jin Xizhi, her uncle-in-law, Cao Mengfei, her aunt, her stepmother, her cousin, Shen Junguan, and a driver, A'fu. They were scheduled to get married at the Tianhexiang Auditorium today (the 26th). However, Ganqing has already married into the Zhou family in Dongshan, which my father knows. My father also agreed to my marriage with Xu. My father gave me 3,000 yuan in silver and gold jewelry. After arriving in Suzhou, my stepmother accompanied me to buy wedding supplies. There are still over 700 yuan left. My father's claim that I secretly stole a 20,000 yuan passbook is not true. Therefore, there was no betrothal gift to save expenses. The matchmaker was Mr. Ran. Female matchmakers are not used in Dongshan customs. She categorically denied that she had eloped. Xu Ganqing testified that he was 31 years old, a native of Dongshan, lived in front of Wangya in Dongshan, and was currently a member of the Wuxian Security Committee. His marriage with Jin Qingxia was agreed upon by both parents. Getting married in Suzhou was also proposed by Jin Xizhi, the woman's father. The woman came to Suzhou with her parents and stepmother. As for my taking a wife of the same surname in Dongshan, it is to continue the Zhou family's lineage. Now that I am marrying Jin, it is to continue my own surname. According to Dongshan customs, it is not bigamy. I don't know how much stuff Jin Qingxia brought when she came to Suzhou. Jin Xizhi, the woman's father, testified that he was a native of Dongshan and lived at No. 73 Wangjiazui in Shanghai. On the 24th of this month, at 12:00 noon, he saw his daughter, Qixia, suddenly disappear. The driver, A'gen, said he saw her carrying things out. He immediately followed with his family to Suzhou and found her at the New Suzhou Hotel in Beiju. He asked her to go back, but she refused. She wanted to marry someone named Xu, which I did not agree to. I was afraid she would run away, so I used soft tactics to keep an eye on her. I called my brother, Zhi Zhi, to Suzhou and reported the case to the detective team. When she ran away this time, after checking the items in the house, in addition to the 20,000 yuan passbook, she also took out a pearl and jade bracelet, a gold ruyi, a rhinestone ring watch, etc. Details are listed in a separate loss report. Her testimony is completely a lie. She was lured out by someone named Xu. Jin Zhi Zhi, the woman's uncle, testified that he was 51 years old and in charge of wrapping in the Dongshan Tongde pawnshop. The rest of his testimony was similar to that of the woman's father. According to the testimonies, the local court, after investigation by Prosecutor Qian that night, released Xu Ganqing on bail pending further investigation. Jin Qingxia was taken back by her uncle, Zhi Zhi. They are scheduled to be summoned for further investigation on Monday.

Robbery and Theft Case Also Recorded: Xiao Zhenjia, the head of the San Tu Township in Maojia City, a county-administered area, was suddenly visited by more than ten bandits at around 10:00 PM last night. Speaking with a Jiangbei accent, they claimed that they only wanted the head of the household and would not steal property. Xiao happened to be out on business and was spared. They robbed clothing and jewelry worth 500 yuan and fled. Also, the home of Fu Zishan, a Hakka resident of Huchuanqiao West He Di, was also robbed that night. Fu woke up from his sleep and escaped from the house. His wife, Sun, was unable to escape and was burned by the thieves with candles. The scene was unbearable. Clothing and jewelry worth about 60 yuan were stolen. The incidents were reported to the Shuangfeng Public Security Branch, which forwarded the report to the county government for investigation.

Wuxi 87

Thugs Send Letters Demanding Thousands of Dollars: Qian Xuefu, a resident of Yangshu in the Sixteenth District, owns a large estate and is one of the richest people in the countryside. His son, Yaliang, runs the Qinyu Silk and Cloth Store in the Beitang Coal Wharf Alley, which has been profitable for years, attracting the attention of thugs. The day before yesterday, Qian Yaliang suddenly received a threatening letter from thugs, stating that they were short of money and borrowing 1,000 yuan and that he must send it to No. 205 Zhonghua Road, Shanghai, within three days, or they would use a gun. Qian was alarmed and reported the information to the Public Security Bureau yesterday, requesting protection. Director Wu ordered detective Yin Chang Xue Furui to send detectives to secretly investigate. Robbery at Night Outside the South Gate: Qiu Qiaofu, a 55-year-old resident of Lu Qingqiao, opposite the Minfeng Silk Factory outside the South Gate of this county, has been making pottery for a living. He is married to Zhou and has three sons. The eldest son, Ronggen, is over thirty years old and has already married. The second son, Mingshan, is twenty years old and married Lanfen, the daughter of Cao Jusheng of Nanmenwan Lane Temple, just on the fifth day of the tenth lunar month of this year. The third son, Rongliang, is only seventeen years old. The family of several people lived happily. Suddenly, at about 12:00 PM yesterday (the 25th), eight or nine bandits, wearing short blue cloth shirts and resembling workers, arrived. One thief was holding a rifle, two thieves were each holding rifles, and the rest were holding axes and other weapons. They used axes to open the window of Mingshan's new house, jumped inside, opened the front door, and rushed in to loot at will. After half an hour, they fled with their loot, which included two gold rings belonging to the bride and groom, and three yuan and two jiao, for a total loss of about 100 yuan.

Changshu 88

Thief Beaten to Death: Beibaoli, about three or four miles from Fushan, is a village where a farmer named Wei Fulin, who is over fifty years old, lives. He has a wife and daughter-in-law, and his family burden is heavy. He also has a fondness for alcohol. Although he has a small amount of farmland, he is always worried about not having enough to live on. The day before yesterday, due to financial difficulties, he went to the home of Su Baosheng nearby to commit theft. He was caught and beaten severely by the crowd. Wei, because of his old age and fondness for alcohol, died after being beaten. The incident was reported to the local town head, who reported it to the Public Security Bureau. The murderer, Su Baosheng, was arrested and reported to the county government. The county sent judicial secretary Ju Yundi and inspector Zhang Renbao to the village for inspection on the 25th.

Provincial Party Committee Comes to Changshu to Investigate Party Affairs: The county representative congress of this county was originally scheduled to be held on the 30th of this month. Some of the representatives from each district have already been elected. However, because the procedures of the congress were not in compliance, some party members filed a complaint with the province. As a result, an order was issued to stop the process. The provincial party department, having learned of the complexity of party affairs here, specially sent committee member Song Yufeng to Changshu for investigation. Song arrived in Changshu on the evening of the 24th. It is said that Song will conduct a detailed investigation, which will take three or four days to complete.

Zhenjiang 89

Kunshan Construction Bureau Chief Wu Ruoyu Escorted to the Province: Jiangsu Province Construction Department Chief Dong Xiujia previously ordered Kunshan County Chief Cheng Ruji to escort Wu Ruoyu, the former construction bureau chief who was in custody for embezzling construction mou tax, to the province for interrogation. After receiving the order, County Chief Cheng, in addition to submitting a reply, yesterday appointed the police captain Luo Qixiang to send a team to escort the criminal to the province by car and transfer him to the Construction Department for transfer to the local court for legal interrogation.

Yangzhou 90

Restoration Party Criminals Escorted to the Province for Interrogation: County Chief Ma Zhenbang, because during the tenure of former County Chief Yang, the Restoration Party criminals Liu Xingyuan and others, who secretly gathered, made noise, gathered crowds, and prepared for riots, were escorted by Yang Qiao's first, second, and third township heads Yang Xiaoyi, Sun Bokuan, and Gao Shuncheng of the Fifth District. Gao Huasong, who was escorted by the Public Security Bureau, has not yet been tried. On the day before yesterday, he proposed a strict interrogation. According to the confessions of Zhang Riqiang, Xi Liren, and Yue Riyong, they, together with the groom Jin Yanglong, knocked and invited the Green Seed Society out. The grooms Jin Yanglong and Zhang Xingyou confessed that they were instructed by Zhang Riqiang to knock and urge people to hold meetings in each village. Gao Huasong claimed that he was a painter and did not participate. The meeting held by Liu Hanqing and others was because he reported that the township head Gao Shunyong had stolen votes in the election, and he did not know the Restoration Party. It was decided that Zhang Riqiang and the other three seemed to be ignorant vagrants, but Liu Xingyuan, although he was a groom, had a tough attitude during the interrogation and was suspected of being reactionary. Gao Huasong was ordered by Yang Zhongyi, a member of the Fifth District's Second Branch, to have the county party department send a letter to the Public Security Bureau to arrest him and take him to the county as a major Restoration Party criminal without cause. The transcripts and examination papers were recorded, and on the 24th, Gao Huasong, Liu Xingyuan, Zhang Xingyou, Jin Yanglong, Yue Riyong, Xi Liren, and Zhang Riqiang were escorted to the province.

Nantong 91

Measures to Rescue the Rural Economy: Recently, the market economy in Tongru Taihaiqi, north of the Yangtze River, has been exhausted, and grain prices have fallen sharply. The rural economy is on the verge of bankruptcy. Currently, Nantong banks are consulting with Provincial Committee Member Xu Wuzhang to entrust the original pawnbrokers in the four villages to allow farmers to pawn fragmented rice. The pawnbrokers will issue pawn tickets as proof. The interest rate is set at 8%, and the term is six months. If the item is not redeemed after the deadline, it can be sold on behalf of the pawner at the market price. Any surplus will still be returned to the mortgagor upon presentation of the ticket.

Solution to the Su Lang Soldier Field: The Tonghai Reclamation Company encroached on 33,900 mu of Su Lang soldier field. After being punished by the Ministry of Military Affairs, the company sued the Haimen County Government, and the court ruled that the soldier field was managed by the company. The Ministry of Military Affairs submitted a request to the Executive Yuan for instructions, ordering the speedy execution of the solution approved by the National Government: 1) The Su Lang two battalions have been reclaiming the field for more than 70 years. The company is still using the original paid reclamation price as shares, which is unfair. The company should be ordered to uniformly pay the price according to the current value. The former soldier field will still belong to the company. 2) If the company is unwilling to fulfill the above method, the company's reclaimed soldier field will be taken back in full and sold separately by auction, or the original tenant will be allowed to pay the price and claim the title to end the matter. Currently, the provincial government has ordered the county government to implement it.

Gaoyou 92

Zhou Luzhuang Robbers Injure People: Zhou Huairen, a farmer in Zhou Luzhuang, the Third District of the county, heard that bandits wanted to kidnap his son, so he temporarily sent his son to the Qi family in Zhangjiazhuang. On the evening of the day before (22nd), more than ten bandits with guns and other weapons broke into the house, tied Zhou Huairen with ropes, and burned his armpits with fire, forcing him to say where his son was. Zhou did not reveal his son's location. The bandits were unable to do anything, so they entered the bedroom and searched it empty, fired a gun, and fled. It is said that the loss was about 200 yuan.

Taixian County 93

Regarding the Prefectural Order to Open Sanli Han: Recently, the Nantong County Chamber of Commerce submitted a report stating that the County Cotton Industry Association and various Salt Reclamation Companies and Yarn Factories had repeatedly reported that cotton from the Yandong area was transported through Sanli Han in Taixian County. However, the entrance to the Han was blocked with wooden stakes, cutting off passage. They requested that the Taixian County Government be instructed to open it to facilitate transportation. This matter was forwarded, and the Taixian County Government was instructed to strictly comply. However, various agencies in the area have not complied with the Prefectural Order and continue to block the passage. As a result, cotton boats traveling through the area must detour an extra one or two hundred li. Furthermore, the river water in Qintong and other places is gradually drying up, making it impossible to reach even after detouring. This will not only affect the cotton industry in Tong County but also the livelihoods of farmers in Yandong and other counties. They requested that the Hai'an agencies under the jurisdiction of Taizhou be instructed to open the Han immediately to facilitate cotton transport. It is now learned that the Construction Department, upon receiving the report, has instructed this county government to comply.

Taizhou 94

Water Police in Fierce Battle with Pirates: The pirates Liang Dachen and Chen San have gathered over a hundred bandits and are hiding in Fuyu Island, Huangyi County. This was detected by the Seventh Water Patrol Team stationed in Jinqing, this county. They dispatched the Fifth and Seventh patrol boats to encircle and suppress them. The bandits resisted stubbornly, and after several hours of fierce fighting, many were killed or injured.

Pinghu 95

Nephew Strangles Uncle: Fan A'da, a farmer in Nanfuxingfang in the urban area, was known for his improper behavior. His uncle, A'hu, had some assets but no descendants, so A'da was to inherit them. Several days ago, A'hu died violently, and it was rumored that uncle and nephew had fought, resulting in an accidental death. After the incident, the neighborhood officer immediately arrested the suspect and sent him to the county government. The investigation has now revealed that A'da coveted his uncle's property and, taking advantage of his early sleep, got into bed and strangled him. He has been interrogated several times and will soon be convicted.

Shaoxing 96

Impersonating a New Young Mistress to Defraud Gold Jewelry: Yao Yu'shi, a woman from San Cai Dian in Shaoxing, used to work as a nanny in the Hu family and had frequent dealings with people in silver shops. Yesterday, Xiang Da'niang, who lived at Bazijiao, accompanied by someone impersonating the new young mistress of the Yao family in Tinghou, invited Yao to Tiancheng Silver Shop on the street to select gold jewelry worth over 600 yuan. The imposter claimed that she needed to take it home to show and would pay immediately. Yao Yu'shi temporarily guaranteed the payment. However, Xiang Tai'niang took the gold jewelry and disappeared elsewhere. Yesterday, Yao reported the incident to the Public Security Bureau, requesting the investigation team to investigate, arrest, and prosecute.

Xiaoshan 97

Worker on Hangzhou-Jiangshan Road Dies in Tragic Fall: On the 23rd, in the early morning, a night train heading from the Jiangbian station to Jinhua on the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Road was carrying over a thousand workers from the Far East Company to work in Jinhua. One of the workers, carrying a bundle of clothes, grabbed onto the train door, intending to board the train. Unexpectedly, the train lurched forward, causing the cars behind to sway. The worker fell and his brains gushed out, resulting in instant death.
