Educational News Headlines

Fujian Province Strictly Implements Compulsory Education 98

Literate People Must Teach Five Illiterate People; Teachers Absent from Duty and Students Absent from Class Will Be Fined. Fuzhou, 26th - The Fujian Provincial Government today passed the Fuzhou City Compulsory Literacy Education Plan, uniting efforts from all sectors of the Party, government, military, and academia to implement it. (1) Every literate citizen is responsible for teaching five illiterate citizens. Those who cannot teach or teach fewer than five people must pay one yuan per person short to hire someone to teach in their place. (2) Teachers absent from duty and students absent from class will be fined three copper coins each time. (3) Elementary school teachers throughout the city will be responsible for inspection and supervision. (4) Illiterate citizens who have not enrolled within the deadline will be fined two jiao per month until they enroll. A Compulsory Literacy Education Committee will be formed, and a propaganda week will be held, along with a city-wide census and literacy test, to prepare for implementation.

High School and Junior High School Cancel Next Semester

Credit System and Elective System 99

No Separate Party Doctrine Course; Optional Second Foreign Language; Published Second Table of Teaching Hours for High School and Junior High School Subjects. Nanjing, 26th - The Ministry of Education recently ordered education departments in all provinces and cities to instruct all high schools and junior high schools under their jurisdiction to implement the teaching and self-study hours for high school and junior high school subjects promulgated by the Ministry, starting next semester. (1) Cancel the credit system. (2) Cancel the elective system. (3) No separate course on Party Doctrine will be established. (4) Self-study hours are specified. In addition, Mongolian, Hui, Tibetan, and second foreign languages may be added as needed in various regions.

Nanjing, 26th - The Ministry of Education announced the Second Table of Weekly Teaching and Self-Study Hours for Each Subject in Junior High School (total weekly teaching hours for each subject): Terms 1, 2, 4, and 6: 35 hours each; Terms 3 and 5: 36 hours each. (Number of weekly self-study hours on campus): Terms 1, 2, 4, and 6: 13 hours each; Terms 3 and 5: 12 hours each. The Ministry of Education announced the Second Table of Weekly Teaching and Self-Study Hours for Each Subject in High School (total weekly teaching hours for each subject): Term 1: 36 hours; Terms 2 and 4: 34 hours each; Term 3: 35 hours; Term 5: 33 hours; Term 6: 31 hours. (Total hours of extracurricular activities and self-study on campus per week): Term 1: 14 hours; Terms 2 and 4: 6 hours each; Term 3: 25 hours; Term 5: 27 hours; Term 6: 29 hours.

Minister of Education Weng to Assume Office Tomorrow 100

Will Determine New Plan after Examining Actual Situation; Expressed to Song Ziwen to Maintain Position Until End of Year. Nanjing, 26th - The new Minister of Education, Weng Wenhao, arrived in Nanjing this morning and is staying at Qian Changxi's residence. He is scheduled to assume office on the 28th.

Special dispatch from Beiping: Minister of Education Weng Wenhao, after repeated entreaties from Premier Song Ziwen, considered the matter and dismissed his intention to resign. Today (24th), Mr. Weng went to the China Education and Culture Foundation at 2:00 PM to bid farewell to Secretary-General Ren Hongjun. At 5:15 PM that afternoon, he took the Pingpu train to Nanjing. Those who saw him off at the station included Jiang Menglin, Wang Zhixiang, Ren Hongjun, Xu Songming, Shen Yinmo, Li Zheng, Hu Shi, Ji Qingzhuo, Wang Yi, Yu Shangchen, and Mei Yiqi, among others, totaling over forty people. Before leaving Beiping, Mr. Weng made the following remarks to reporters:

Weng's Remarks Before Leaving Beiping: I have repeatedly declined the position of Minister of Education, but to no avail. Premier Song (Ziwen) wants me to maintain my position at the Ministry of Education, so I can only maintain it temporarily. The duration will be until the end of December, at which time I will resign and return to Beiping. My ambition lies in studying geology; I have never left geological work in the past twenty years. Since Premier Song has allowed me to maintain my position until the Third Plenary Session, I can temporarily assume the duties of Minister of Education. The education budget is difficult, and the pending issues at Peking University have not been resolved. The education situation in the South also needs to be investigated after arriving in Nanjing. Therefore, all plans must be determined after inspecting the actual situation in Nanjing. I have no comments at this time.

Telegram Reply to Song Ziwen: To Premier Song Ziwen of the Nanjing Executive Yuan: I received your telegram of the 16th. For twenty years, I have never left geological work, and my previous resignation was sincere. Vice Minister Qian relayed your intentions, allowing me to maintain my position until the Third Plenary Session, which is not far off. Would frequent changes be more troublesome? If deemed necessary, I will come immediately to maintain the position temporarily, but I will resign and leave Nanjing by the end of December, regardless of whether a replacement is found. I hope you will consider this carefully. Respectfully, Weng Wenhao.

Legislative Yuan Passes Normal School and Vocational School Laws 101

The Legislative Yuan passed the Normal School Law and the Vocational School Law at its 214th meeting on the 26th. The summaries are as follows:

(1) Normal School Law

Article 1: Normal schools shall, in accordance with the educational objectives and implementation policies of the Republic of China, cultivate healthy elementary school teachers through rigorous physical and mental training.

Article 2: Normal schools may establish special normal classes and kindergarten normal classes as affiliated programs.

Article 3: The duration of study in normal schools is three years, one year for special normal classes, and two or three years for kindergarten normal classes.

Article 4: Normal schools shall be established by provinces or municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan. However, based on local needs, they may also be established by counties or jointly by two or more counties.

Article 5: Normal schools established by provinces, municipalities, or counties are provincial, municipal, or county normal schools. Normal schools jointly established by two or more counties are joint normal schools of those counties.

Article 6: The establishment, modification, and closure of normal schools, if established by provinces or municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan, shall be reported by the provincial or municipal education administrative agencies to the Ministry of Education for record. If established by counties or municipalities, it shall be submitted through the education department for approval and forwarded to the Ministry of Education for record.

Article 7: The teaching subjects, curriculum standards, and internship regulations of normal schools and their special normal classes and kindergarten normal classes shall be determined by the Ministry of Education. Normal schools shall establish vocational subjects based on local needs.

Article 8: Textbooks and teaching materials for normal schools and their special normal classes and kindergarten normal classes shall be those edited or approved by the Ministry of Education.

Article 9: Normal schools may establish affiliated elementary schools. Those with affiliated kindergarten normal classes may also establish kindergartens.

Article 10: Normal schools shall have one principal to manage school affairs. The provincial normal school principal shall be nominated by the education department from qualified personnel and appointed after being approved by the provincial government committee. The municipal normal school directly under the Executive Yuan shall be selected by the municipal education administrative agency from qualified personnel and submitted to the municipal government for approval. The county and city normal school principal shall be selected by the county and city governments from qualified personnel and submitted to the education department for approval. In addition to teaching courses at the school, the principal shall not hold other positions. The appointment of the principals of the aforementioned normal schools shall be submitted by the provincial and municipal education administrative agencies to the Ministry of Education for record on a regular basis.

Article 11: Normal school teachers shall be appointed by the principal and shall be full-time. However, in special circumstances, part-time teachers may be hired, but their number shall not exceed one-fourth of the total number of teachers. Normal school staff shall be appointed by the principal and shall be submitted to the competent education administrative agency for record.

Article 12: Regulations for the appointment of normal school principals and teachers shall be determined by the Ministry of Education.

Article 13: Applicants for normal schools and their kindergarten normal classes must have graduated from public or registered private junior high schools. Applicants for special normal classes must have graduated from public or registered private senior high schools or senior vocational schools. All applicants must pass the entrance examination.

Article 14: Students of normal schools and their special normal classes and kindergarten normal classes who complete their studies, finish their internships, and pass their examinations shall be awarded graduation certificates by the school.

Article 15: Normal schools and their special normal classes and kindergarten normal classes shall not collect tuition fees.

Article 16: The regulations of normal schools and the service regulations of normal school graduates shall be determined by the Ministry of Education.

Article 17: This law shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

(2) Vocational School Law

Article 1: Vocational schools shall, in accordance with the educational objectives and implementation policies of the Republic of China, cultivate young people's knowledge of life and production skills.

Article 2: Vocational schools are divided into junior vocational schools and senior vocational schools.

Article 3: The establishment of vocational schools shall be based on a single department in principle, but in special circumstances, several departments may be established.

Article 4: Junior vocational schools shall admit elementary school graduates or those engaged in vocational work with equivalent qualifications. The duration of study is one to three years. Senior vocational schools shall admit junior high school graduates or those with equivalent qualifications. The duration of study is three years. Those who admit elementary school graduates or those with equivalent qualifications shall have a duration of study of five or six years. Vocational schools shall admit students only after they have passed the entrance examination.

Article 5: Vocational schools may establish various vocational supplementary classes depending on the circumstances.

Article 6: Vocational schools shall be named senior or junior vocational schools of a certain department according to the departments they establish. Those that concurrently establish two or more departments shall be called senior or junior vocational schools. Those that jointly establish both levels shall be called vocational schools.

Article 7: Vocational schools shall be established by provinces or municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan. However, based on local needs, they may be established by counties or jointly by two or more counties. Private individuals or groups may also establish vocational schools.

Article 8: Vocational schools established by provinces, municipalities, or counties are provincial, municipal, or county vocational schools. Vocational schools jointly established by two or more counties are joint vocational schools of those counties. Vocational schools established by private individuals or groups are private vocational schools.

Article 9: The establishment, modification, or closure of district vocational schools, if established by provinces or municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan, shall be reported by the provincial or municipal education administrative agencies to the Ministry of Education for record. The rest shall be submitted to the provincial or municipal education administrative agencies for approval and forwarded to the Ministry of Education for record.

Article 10: The teaching subjects, equipment standards, curriculum standards, and internship regulations of vocational schools at all levels shall be determined by the Ministry of Education.

Article 11: Vocational schools shall have one principal to manage school affairs. The provincial vocational school principal shall be nominated by the education department from qualified personnel and appointed after being approved by the provincial government committee. The municipal vocational school directly under the Executive Yuan shall be selected by the municipal education administrative agency from qualified personnel and submitted to the municipal government for approval. The county and city vocational school principal shall be selected by the county and city governments from qualified personnel and submitted to the education department for approval and shall not hold concurrent positions. The appointment of the principals of the aforementioned vocational schools shall be submitted by the provincial and municipal education administrative agencies to the Ministry of Education for record on a regular basis. The principal of a private vocational school shall be selected and appointed by the board of directors from qualified personnel and shall be submitted to the competent education administrative agency for record.

Article 12: Vocational school teachers shall be appointed by the principal and shall be full-time. However, in special circumstances, part-time teachers may be hired. Vocational school staff shall be appointed by the principal and shall be submitted to the competent education administrative agency for record.

Article 13: Regulations for the appointment of vocational school principals and teachers shall be determined by the Ministry of Education.

Article 14: Students of vocational schools who complete their studies, finish their internships, and pass their examinations shall be awarded graduation certificates by the school.

Article 15: Vocational schools shall not collect tuition fees in principle.

Article 16: The regulations of vocational schools shall be determined by the Ministry of Education.

Article 17: This law shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

Truly 18,000 People; Never Before Seen at a Football Match; Yesterday's Match Was Truly a Grand Event, Unprecedented in Chinese Sports History. Bird's-Eye View of the Situation 113

Hong Kong Team Takes Full Offensive; Shanghai Team Loses After Leading. In the overall situation of the game, the Hong Kong team dominated everywhere. The second half was almost entirely dominated by Hong Kong.

First Half Report 114

Hong Kong Team's Presence on the Field

Applause erupted as the two teams entered the field. Shanghai kicked off, but the ball was blocked by Pai Duo and retreated. Ba De Lai followed the ball and advanced, but Shi Du Ke stumbled, almost causing a disaster at the start. Subsequently, the Hong Kong forwards' sharp and brave offensives were evident within twenty minutes. The Shanghai team's attack saw Bao Er Dun receive a pass from the rear and rush forward, reaching the goal, but he and Tu Na both missed. Chen Jiaqiu dribbled around on the left and right, showing great power, but he held the ball for too long and was intercepted by Bei Lishi. Such an opportunity made people sigh for Shanghai.

Zheng Shaokang's Wonderful Header for the First Goal. Hong Kong launched a counterattack, and Zheng Shaokang headed in a corner kick, which was well-placed and almost scored. Pai Duo took a free kick in the middle of the field and shot it fiercely towards the goal. Zhou Xianyan扑ed it out, causing a sensation in the audience. Amidst the dangerous waves, an unexpected disaster occurred. Ba De Lai got a corner kick, and as the ball was about to fall, Zheng Shaokang, a surprise soldier on the right wing, accurately judged the ball and headed it in at that moment. Hong Kong took the lead, twenty minutes after the opening.

12-Yard Penalty Allows Shanghai to Tie the Score. Five minutes after Hong Kong scored, Bao Er Dun received a ball from Hei Tan on the right. The opportunity was very good, but he lifted his foot too late. The goalkeeper was prepared and punched the ball out. The ball fell in front of Hei Tan, and Tu Na kicked it, but Hong Kong's central defender Pai Duo tried to stop it but accidentally touched the ball with his hand within the penalty area. The referee ordered a penalty kick, and Ga Xu rushed up and kicked it in. Hong Kong and Shanghai each scored a goal, and Xu Yahui was injured in an instant.

Endless Thrills for the Shanghai Team

The two sides attacked and defended, neither side having the advantage. Ba De Lai shot directly at the goal from the left wing, and Zhou Xianyan showed panic and almost lost the goal. Sun Zhongshun suddenly lifted a ball, Huang Meishun passed it to Ba De Lai again, and Ba shot with all his strength, but Zhou Xianyan urgently saved it, showing the magic of the iron gate. Sun Jinshun got the ball from Ba De Lai, Shi Du Ke was careless and made a mistake, but fortunately He Lei rushed to save the situation with a kick, revealing the thrilling nature of the Shanghai team.

Extreme Danger Brings Good Fortune, Shanghai Takes the Lead

Danger turned into good fortune. Bao Er Dun passed to Kai Zhi, Kai Zhi set his foot and sent the ball from the right straight to the left corner. Hei Tan took advantage of the situation to shoot and create a corner kick. Hei Tan's accurate landing point became a scramble in front of the goal. Ga Xu took the opportunity to kick, and Bao Er Dun watched coldly and sent the ball rolling into the goal, putting Shanghai ahead 2-1.

Zheng Shaokang Scores a Wonderful Second Goal

One wave rises, and another comes. The speed of the changing situation is endless. Two minutes after scoring the third goal, Hong Kong used lightning tactics. Sun Jinshun flew the ball to Zheng Shaokang, who shot it from the right corner to the left corner. With Ba De Lai, Li Ning, and Shi Du Ke losing sight of each other, the ball flew to the right corner again. Shaokang shot it in, and the speed of his passing was incredibly beautiful.

Bao Er Dun Misses an Opportunity

Although Bao Er Dun missed an opportunity, Kai Zhi advanced along the right side, and Bei Lishi kicked it out of bounds. He Lei threw it in, and Qiu Jia lifted it and passed it to Tu Na. Tu passed it to the left, and Chen Zhenhe flew up and scored in the absence of anyone guarding him, putting the Shanghai team ahead 3-2.

A Carbon Copy

Five minutes before the end of the first half, Hong Kong center forward Huo Wei shot straight at the goal in front of the goal, and Zhou Xianyan's wonderful save was praised. Ba De Lai got the ball on the left and passed it to the right. Li Ning and Shi Du Ke both stumbled at the same time. Huang Meishun shot fiercely at the goal, and the iron gate fell with a bang, but fortunately, it was still thrown out. Ba De Lai could have shot at an empty goal, but he flew the ball far away. Like Bao Er Dun, he missed an opportunity. Thus, it can be said that Bao Er Dun treated the audience to a miss.

Little Hei Tan's Sneak Attack Breaks the Hong Kong Army

What is lost on the east coast is gained on the west. Although Bao Er Dun missed an opportunity, Kai Zhi advanced along the right side, and Bei Lishi kicked it out of bounds. He Lei threw it in, and Qiu Jia passed it to Tu Na. Tu passed it to the left, and Chen Zhenhe flew up and scored in the absence of anyone guarding him, putting the Shanghai team ahead 3-2.

No Coincidence

Ba De Lai received the ball on the left and passed it to the right. Li Ning and Shi Du Ke stumbled at the same time. Second Half Situation 115

丨Hong Kong Troops Swift and Unforeseen丨

Lemon took a break to reorganize. Due to Xu Yahui's foot injury, Shanghai placed him on the left wing, Chen Zhenhe moved into the left inside, and Tui Na retreated to the Asian position. Hong Kong kicked off. Unexpectedly, within just two minutes, the Hong Kong team launched a massive offensive, reaching the front of the goal. Huang Meishun shot and scored, breaching the iron gate three times. Hong Kong tied the score at 3-3. Tui Na was also injured.

Hong Kong Team Wins the Interport Silver Cup (Photo by Xinsheng News Agency)

丨Huo Wei's Header Seals the Victory丨

The Hong Kong team's momentum surged. The Shanghai team's injury-riddled and chaotic situation was exposed. Their offensive power was gone, leaving them at the mercy of Hong Kong. The ball's trajectory was entirely controlled by the Hong Kong team. After fifteen minutes of dull and uninspired fighting, the victor was finally decided. Pai Duo sent a pass to the left corner. Badley flew up and crossed the ball. An enemy flew in from the sky, catching Zhou’s iron gate by surprise. Huo Wei flew in and headed the ball into the net. This seventh goal ultimately determined the victory for Hong Kong over Shanghai.

丨Final Struggles End in Vain丨

The Shanghai team became a spent force. Their offense was ineffective, and their defense was in dire straits. In the final ten minutes, Ya Xu repeatedly tried his best to advance, but the army had been shattered, and he was fighting a losing battle. Kai Zhi's corner kick and He Lei's free kick were Shanghai's last hopes and struggles, but they all came to naught. The entire Hong Kong team retreated to defend strictly. As night fell, the Shanghai team watched as the Hong Kong team took the silver cup away.

Hong Kong Team's Wonderful Skills 116

The forwards are agile and surprisingly nimble, the midfield is strong, and the goalkeeper is inferior. The Hong Kong team's victory was by no means accidental. Their football skills are indeed superior. The forwards' agility, the accuracy of their shots, and the speed of their cooperation are all wonderfully indescribable. Only Huang Meishun, being unfamiliar with the forward position, was sometimes seen lagging behind Zheng Shaokang on the right wing, much like Cao Guicheng. Right winger Badley's several crosses deserve great credit. These five tigers are both loved and feared. The midfield is also strong, and although the defenders were not particularly outstanding, they did not make any major mistakes. The only shortcoming was the goalkeeper's lack of stability.

Shanghai Team Greatly Diminished 117

The forwards lacked attacking and shooting ability, and the defense showed signs of wavering. The Shanghai team's failure can be attributed to certain causes. The strong defenders actually showed signs of wavering. Zhou Xianyan's defense in the rear was diminished by Li Ning. Stoke was mediocre. Xu Yahui and He Lei were also not outstanding. Xu may have been affected by his position. The forwards lacked any cooperation. Balton's center forward was inexplicably sluggish. His slow movements caused them to miss countless opportunities. This was their greatest weakness. Chen Zhenhe was watched closely by Duncan, making it difficult for him to move. Of the entire team, only Ya Xu remained consistently unyielding. The selection committee should bear the responsibility for this failure. When the Shanghai team goes to Hong Kong for the New Year, they must be completely refreshed.

The Team Leader's Honor 118

Mo Yinghuan Discusses Hong Kong Team Strategy

This is the first time that the Hong Kong team has been led by a Chinese team leader and broken the Interport record in Shanghai. Mo Yinghuan's fortune is also considered one of the reasons for the victory. After the match, Mr. Mo said that the Hong Kong team's tactics were different in the first and second halves. The first half focused on attacking the right, and the second half focused on attacking the left. He humbly said that Shanghai's defeat was due to too many injuries.

Ministry of Education Commends Jinan University 126

Faculty and Staff Work Hard, Students Study Peacefully. Nanjing, 26th Telegram: The Ministry of Education, in order to improve university education, sent personnel to inspect Jinan University. It was found that the school had suffered many losses in buildings and equipment since the Shanghai incident, but it was able to gradually restore its former appearance in a short period of time. The students were able to study peacefully after being screened, and the faculty and staff also worked hard. The Ministry of Education praised this as rare. Yesterday, the school was instructed on several matters that should be improved: 1. Provision of funding for library equipment in accordance with regulations. 2. The Chinese and English departments of the School of Liberal Arts should be divided. 3. There are too many part-time teachers in the middle school department, and methods should be improved. 4. Efforts should be made to establish a Nanyang Museum in the Department of Nanyang and American Cultural Affairs.

National Mandarin Chinese Performance Competition to be Held 127

Report Before November 30th, Competition on December 3rd and 4th. In order to promote Mandarin Chinese education, the National Mandarin Chinese Education Promotion Association is holding the first National Mandarin Chinese Performance Competition in Shanghai. The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education has issued a notice to all municipal public and private elementary school students to participate in the competition. It is heard that the competition will be limited to one-act plays for the time being, and each script must not exceed five minutes. The competition is divided into two groups, A and B, with grades 3 and 4 of elementary school in Group A and grades 1 and 2 of advanced elementary school in Group B. Participating schools must send the names, birthplaces, ages, and levels of the participants, along with the scripts, to the association's office at No. 98 Pingle Lane, Xizang Road, before November 30th. The Group A competition will begin at 1:00 PM on December 3rd, and the Group B competition will begin at 1:00 PM on December 4th. The judges will be appointed by the staff of the Bureau of Education and the association's directors.

Liu Chongjie Discusses Recent Diplomatic Situation 130

Ultimately, the People of the Country Must Work Hard Themselves. Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs Liu Chongjie Arrived in Shanghai from Beijing Yesterday Morning. A Reporter from the Huadong News Agency Interviewed Mr. Liu at the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Was Granted an Interview. When Asked About the Recent Situation of the League of Nations' Handling of the Sino-Japanese Manchurian Case, the Attitudes of Various Related Countries, and Our Country's Recent Position, Mr. Liu Answered in Detail and Reported on the Progress of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Recent Negotiations on the Sino-French Vietnam Trade Agreement and the Sino-Brazilian Trade Agreement. The Conversation Is Recorded as Follows:

The League of Nations Situation: We Can See Everything About the Recent Situation of the League of Nations in the Newspapers. The League of Nations Is Now Handling the Sino-Japanese Dispute and Has Decided to Hand It Over to the Nineteen-Member Committee for Discussion at a Special Assembly. Some People Believe That Japan Is Strongly Opposed to This, So They Believe That the Trend Is Beneficial to Our Side, While Others Believe That the League of Nations Is Just Delaying and Will Ultimately Produce No Results. In Fact, Such Optimistic Hopes and Pessimistic Disappointments Are Both Unhelpful. Dependence Is Not Expected, and Negativity Is Not a Good Policy. In Summary, the League of Nations' Handling of This Case Will Eventually Have a Significant Outcome, or It Will Be the Fundamental Failure of the League of Nations. Do We Not See That the League of Nations Has Declared That It Will Ultimately Maintain the League of Nations? If the League of Nations Handles the Sino-Japanese Case and Ultimately Produces No Results, Then It Will Go Back on Its Word.

Unity in Foreign Affairs: Now Is the Time for the League of Nations to Maintain the League of Nations. We Certainly Hope That the League of Nations Will Have a Fair Resolution, but We Must Not Rely on It. The Central Authorities Are Now Making Efforts to Foreign Affairs, and All Sectors of the Country Are Doing the Same. At This Time, the Three Representatives Yan, Gu, and Guo Are Making Great Efforts to Negotiate on the International Stage. Their Task Is Extremely Important. All Our Countrymen Should Warmly Support One Representative's Efforts to Serve the Country. If the Whole Country Is United in Foreign Affairs, Then the Victory of Diplomacy Can Be Expected. Regarding Japan's Tanaka Cabinet Memorandum, Japanese Representative Matsuoka and Our Representative Gu Had a Fierce Debate on This Matter. Representative Gu Has Already Provided Strong Evidence of Matsuoka's Own Writings and Recent Facts, and Former Minister Shi Has Also Made a Statement. In This Regard, I Believe That Everything Will Ultimately Be Proven by Facts. If Japan Denies That the Tanaka Memorandum Was Made by Japan Itself, Then Why Are Today's Actions So Consistent with the Contents?

International Trends: The Current International Situation Is Focused on the Dispute in the Far East. The Concerns of Various Countries About This Are Different, but the War Debt Problem Between Europe and the United States Has Also Had Repeated Twists and Turns Recently. Therefore, It May Inevitably Affect the Dispute in the Far East. However, Britain and France Have Always Been Keen on Peace and Are Powerful Members of the League of Nations. They Should Not Change Their Policies. As for the United States, Although Roosevelt Has Been Reelected as President, Observing His Recent Diplomatic Trends, He Is Also Unlikely to Change His Far Eastern Policy. In Addition, the Resumption of Relations Between the United States and Russia Was Previously Rumored to Be Possible. How Is It Progressing Now? The News Is Very Quiet. Our Country's Resumption of Relations with Russia Has Also Tended to Stagnate Recently. On the Japanese Side, Before the League of Nations General Assembly Was Held, They Attempted to Cooperate with Russia in Order to Threaten Various Countries, but They Were Also Unsuccessful. Now, World Opinion on Japan Has Gradually Become Clear, So Japan Is Quite Vocal About Withdrawing from the League of Nations. Whether This Matter Can Be Realized and What Kind of Plans Japan Will Have in the Future, We Can Ignore Them. We Only Know That We Must Cooperate with the International Community from a Position of Justice. We Only Know That Power Can Never Suppress Justice. Therefore, No Matter What, We Must Strive Together Internally and Externally at This Time.

Revising Trade Agreements: In Addition to Devoting Itself to Dealing with the League of Nations, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Has Also Been Working on All Government Affairs, Such as Revising the Sino-French Vietnam Trade Agreement. It Has Recently Consulted with French Minister Wei Lide Several Times. Currently, Only the Tax Items of Both Parties Are Still Under Discussion and Should Be Completed Soon. The Two Governments of China and France Approved This Trade Agreement Long Ago. The Reason Why It Has Not Been Realized Sooner Is the Tax Problem. In Addition, the Sino-Brazilian Trade Agreement Has Also Been Discussed and Has Come to a Conclusion. The Brazilian Minister Is Now Asking His Government for Instructions and Should Also Be Resolved Soon.

Japanese Naval Actions in China 132

Expanding the Yangtze River Fleet: A large contingent of naval personnel arrives in Shanghai; Commander Sakonji Returns Home; New Recruits Arrive in Shanghai. During this month, the Japanese Navy, taking advantage of officer rotations, has been vigorously expanding its Marine Corps and Yangtze River Fleet. The number of Marines in Shanghai and Hankou has increased to 3,200, organized in a manner similar to the army. Furthermore, reinforcements have been added to the warships of the First Overseas Dispatch Fleet. 450 soldiers were transferred from the Sasebo Naval Corps, transported to Shanghai by the special service ship Aotaka, arriving in Wusong yesterday afternoon. Around 3 PM, they entered the port and disembarked at the Osaka Wharf in Yangshupu. After arriving in Shanghai, Commander Sakano assigned them to serve on various ships, and they were transported to Nanjing and Hankou on Sino-Japanese river steamers to replenish forces.

Commander Returns to Japan: Rear Admiral Sakonji, commander of the Third Fleet, is scheduled to return to Japan at 3 PM today on the flagship Izumo from the Huishan Wharf. Commander Sakano and Captain Sugita of the Japanese Navy in Shanghai, Staff Officer Shima, Rear Admiral Tashiro, and consuls will all be present at the wharf to see him off. Representatives of the Japanese community and 200 elementary school students will also present flags to bid him farewell.

Admiral Yonai Arrives in Shanghai: Rear Admiral Yonai, the newly appointed commander of the Third Fleet, telegraphed Shanghai yesterday stating that he will depart from Sasebo on the flagship Izumo on December 4th and arrive in Shanghai around noon on the 6th to take over as the new commander. On the 7th and 8th, he will call on the Mayor of our city, naval authorities, and visit the commanders of various foreign fleets in Shanghai.

Military Equipment Delivered: During the 128 Incident, many of the Yangtze River warships participated in the fighting, consuming a significant amount of ammunition. Replenishment has been provided by the Ministry of the Navy. Now, a large shipment of military equipment has arrived from Japan, transported to Shanghai yesterday by the Aotaka. It includes a large quantity of rifles, bullets, machine guns, hand grenades, and bombs, totaling over 100 tons, which were all unloaded at the Osaka Wharf military equipment warehouse yesterday. This equipment is designated for the various ships of the First Overseas Dispatch Fleet.

Increase in Warships: Japanese warships on the upper reaches of the Yangtze River have been designated: Atami, Futami, and Ooe will be sent to Sichuan. The four ships of the 15th Squadron - Ashi, Ogi, Fuji, and Susuki - are confirmed to leave Shanghai on Thursday to return to Japan. Four destroyers from the 27th Squadron will arrive in Shanghai on Saturday to be stationed in Shanghai. On the Yangtze River from Hankou to Nanjing and Zhenjiang, the following ships are assigned: Tenryu, Kamikaze, Unazuki, Katata, Tado, Hira, Fushimi, Toba, Momoyana, Hinoki, and Kasagi. In Hunan, the Sumida, Izumo, and Ataka are all departing from Shanghai. A total of 21 warships are deployed on the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River.

Navy Changes Flags: The Third Fleet Command of the Japanese Navy stationed in Shanghai has received instructions from the Ministry of the Navy that the flags of naval warships and destroyers have been revised with a new design, called the Hinomaru Flag. The new flags were distributed to various warships by the command headquarters after being sent from Japan yesterday. It was decided that all ships would uniformly change to the new Hinomaru-style flags on November 1st. All foreign warships were notified to take note.

Aviation Association Raises Funds for "Boy Scout" Airplane 133

Since Japanese aircraft bombed Shanghai, the people of the country have all felt the need to prepare aviation as the only weapon to deal with the brutal Japanese aggression in the future, especially the city's Boy Scouts who have served on the battlefield and personally experienced the threat of Japanese aircraft. Therefore, since the China Aviation Construction Association solicited members, the City Boy Scout Council organized a Boy Scout recruitment team, promoting Tong Xingbai, Wang Gang, and Leng Yunqiao as captain and vice-captains, and promoting Pan Gongzhan, Xia Huanxin, Yu Kuiyuan, Qu Yue, Xu Zicheng, Zhang Xunfang, and Luo Lie as recruitment committee members. They plan to raise funds for a "Boy Scout" airplane to address the national crisis, and have scheduled a meeting for 7:00 PM tonight at the Moore Memorial Church to discuss the fundraising procedures.

Geng Jizhou's Troops Telegraph Recapture of Xintaizi Station 134

Rebel Army under Fu Surrenders with their Troops; Our Army Captures Enemy Weapons and Ammunition.

According to the Far East News Agency, Yang Yijie and Cao Fengxun, representatives of Geng Jizhou, Commander-in-Chief of the Liaoxi Volunteer Army stationed in Shanghai, received a telegram yesterday from the army's Beijing office reporting the recapture of Xintaizi Station. The telegram reads as follows: (omitted above) After retreating from Jiguan Mountain, our army under Zhou Zhenbang immediately fortified their defenses, incorporating over 5,000 local militia members. They purchased over 300 warhorses and formed a cavalry regiment to move towards Tieling. On the 19th, they clashed with Zhang Haipeng's rebel forces at Bali Village. The rebel force of only over 500 was immediately surrounded by our forces. That evening, led by Regiment Commander Chuan Chang, the entire force surrendered, bringing with them 17 machine guns, eight cannons, and hundreds of thousands of rounds of ammunition. On the morning of the 20th, they all moved towards the Lalinzi area. Hundreds of local villagers carrying rifles and farm tools came to join them. On the 22nd, they advanced from Dakang Village and occupied Xintaizi Station, engaging in fierce fighting with over 700 Japanese guards, killing over 40 of them and routing the rest. On the morning of the 23rd, the enemy's Matsuda Regiment reinforced from Hutai, engaging in fierce fighting for a day and night. The enemy was unable to withstand and retreated again. In this battle, our army captured countless enemy weapons and ammunition. In the evening, the enemy and rebels attacked from the north and south. Our army divided to counterattack.

He Minhun Appoints Yan Bowei as Commander-in-Chief of the Sixth Route Army for National Salvation 135

About to Depart North to Assume Post

He Minhun, Military Chairman of the Jehol National Salvation Army, recently appointed his representative in Shanghai, Yan Bowei, as the Commander-in-Chief of the Sixth Route Army of the National Salvation Army. The force consists of three divisions, totaling over 20,000 soldiers. Now that Mr. Yan has received his appointment, he is scheduled to depart from Shanghai within days, carrying cotton clothing, military supplies, etc., to assume his command post. It is reported that Mr. Yan is a graduate of the Baoding Military Academy and has held important military and political positions.

Zhu Hexiang to Visit Southeast Asia the Day After Tomorrow 136

Inspect Conditions at Various Consulates

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs, due to the need to rectify the conditions at various consulates in Southeast Asia, has specially appointed Zhu Hexiang, Director of the International Affairs Department of the Ministry, to conduct an inspection. After receiving the order, Mr. Zhu came to Shanghai to prepare for the voyage. It is now learned that Mr. Zhu has purchased a ship ticket and is scheduled to depart at 2 PM on the 29th on the British ship Komarin, first going to Southeast Asia and the Philippines for a period of four months. His secretary, Zhou Bofu, etc., will accompany him.

Important Tasks: It is reported that his important tasks are: 1. Whether the consuls-general and consuls in various places can faithfully implement the ministry's orders; 2. Whether they can fulfill their responsibilities in protecting overseas Chinese; 3. Whether they have statistics and plans regarding commercial conditions; 4. Whether they can maintain harmonious relationships with overseas Chinese and whether there are any illegal or private dealings; 5. Whether the staff within the consulates can cooperate harmoniously and whether they can invigorate their work; 6. Whether they can effectively liaise with local officials and consuls of other countries in the host country; 7. Whether the overseas Chinese in each area are harmonious and whether there are bad habits such as frequent fighting. A brief biography is recorded below:

Zhu's Biography: Zhu Hexiang, courtesy name Fengqian, is from Baoshan County, Jiangsu Province. He graduated from Fudan Public School in Wusong and Aurora College in Shanghai, holding a Bachelor of Law and a Doctor of Political Science and Diplomacy from the Free University of Brussels. He has successively served as a Principal Clerk, Section Chief, Secretary, Counselor, and Director in the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and as a Recorded Plenipotentiary Minister. He has also served as the Acting Minister of Foreign Affairs, and concurrently as a Professor of Law at Peking University, a member of the Legal Rights Discussion Committee, a specialist member and Director of Affairs of the Sino-Russian Conference, and Director-General of the General Affairs Office of the Special Customs Conference. He is currently the Director of the International Affairs Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs.

Waterway Expert Dickson Goes to Yichang 137

Will Use Explosives to Blast Kongling Shoals.

The "China Press" reports that Kongling Shoals, located 33 miles upstream from Yichang, stands tall in the middle of the river and has always been one of the Yangtze River's dangerous shoals. Every winter, when the water level drops, the river channel is only navigable on the edges, and due to the swift currents, accidents are most likely to occur. To ensure the safety of navigation on the upper reaches of the river, the National Government has established a Kongling Shoals Committee to plan for the improvement of the waterway. Preliminary surveys began a year ago, and it has been determined that the reefs of the shoals can be leveled with explosives. Now, expert Dickson has been hired to conduct a review together with Everest of the Yichang Customs River Patrol, to suggest plans to improve the waterway. Dickson set off from Shanghai yesterday morning (24th) to travel via Hankou to Yichang. The shipping industry in this port is paying close attention to this great plan of the National Government because it is of great relevance to the shipping industry.

Sino-Belgian Geng Commission Met Yesterday 138

Decided to Hold a National University Thesis Award

To announce test questions before January 1 next year.

The Chinese delegation of the Sino-Belgian Geng Commission held a meeting of the Chinese delegation at 4 PM yesterday at the Chu residence on Avenue Albert. The meeting was attended by Chairman Chu Minyi, Commission members Rong Pu, Li Zhaohuan, Zhu Shiquan, and Kong Lihang, and observers Liu Xichang, Nong Ruhui, and Tian Shouchang. The meeting discussed holding a national university thesis award and resolved that the commission would allocate 3,000 yuan annually as prize money, and formulate prize regulations and detailed rules. A review committee was organized, consisting of the previously hired question-setting experts. The test questions will be announced before January 1 next year, and a letter will be sent to the Central Party Headquarters and the Ministries of Education and Railways for record. The prize thesis regulations and detailed rules are recorded below.

Sino-Belgian Geng Commission University Thesis Award Regulations Article 1: This commission allocates 3,000 silver dollars annually as the Chinese University Thesis Award to encourage academic research. Article 2: This award is divided into several types, each with several levels. The commission will set essay questions and select those with truly original ideas and value, awarding prizes separately based on the results of the evaluation. In addition to the prize money, an honorary certificate may be given. Article 3: Those applying for this thesis must be graduating students from a legally registered university or independent college in the country, and their thesis must be related to their major subject. Article 4: The types and categories of theses and the distribution of prize money shall be determined by the Chinese delegation of this commission before soliciting essays each year. Article 5: The commission shall hire experts to form a committee to handle the proposition and evaluation of the theses. Article 6: The text of the thesis shall be in Chinese, but it may also be in English, German, or French, provided that a Chinese translation is attached. Article 5: If the expert committee evaluates the theses of each department and finds that none is worthy of a certain type or level of award, the Chinese delegation of this commission may retain the award for that type or level as an accumulation of the award. Article 8: The above accumulation fund shall be used by the commission, but still limited to encouraging academic research. Article 9: Detailed rules for the implementation of these regulations shall be determined separately. Article 10: These regulations may be amended by the Chinese delegation of this commission.

Provisional Detailed Rules for the Sino-Belgian Geng Commission University Thesis Award Article 1: These detailed rules are formulated in accordance with Article 9 of the University Thesis Award Regulations of this commission. Article 2: As stipulated in Article 1 of the University Thesis Award Regulations of this commission, the prize is divided into six types, each with three levels: Level A, 300 yuan; Level B, 150 yuan; Level C, 50 yuan. The levels shall be discussed and decided by the commission according to the results of the thesis evaluation and awarded separately. Article 3: Each academic year, the commission shall rotate and designate six departments from the departments specified in Article 6 of the university regulations of the Ministry of Education, and hire experts to propose topics and announce the essay solicitation before January 1. Article 4: Each thesis must be sent by the president of the university or the dean of the independent college where the applicant is located to the secretariat of this commission before May 15 of the same year, along with a written certificate stating the author's name, place of origin, age, gender, class, department, and the name and academic qualifications of their advisor. Article 5: The thesis evaluation committee shall submit the evaluation results along with each thesis to the secretariat of this commission within one month of receiving the theses, for review and announcement by the Chinese delegation. Article 6: A list of reference books must be attached at the end of the thesis. If Chinese is used, the original foreign professional terms should be attached in detail. Article 7: Each award and honorary certificate shall be sent by the Chinese delegation of this commission to the school of the award recipient for forwarding. Article 8: This commission may publish each winning thesis. Article 10: All theses, whether they win an award or not, will not be returned. Article 10: These detailed rules may be amended by the Chinese delegation of this commission at any time if there are any matters not covered.

Liu Peiquan, General Manager of China Aviation Corporation, Resigns and is Approved 139

Successor to be Elected by the Board of Directors. Since taking office in May of this year, Mr. Liu Peiquan, General Manager of China Aviation Corporation, has put great effort into developing the company's business, such as planning the Shanghai-Qingdao air route and establishing aviation tourism, which has been praised by the American shareholders. Now, Mr. Liu has other important matters, so he submitted his resignation to the Ministry of Communications. Minister of Communications Zhu Jiaju, recognizing Mr. Liu's firm determination to leave, specially approved it. This approval order arrived in Shanghai yesterday, and the company is rushing to complete the handover. It is reported that the selection of the new general manager must be elected by the board of directors. The representatives previously sent by the Ministry of Communications, Jianping, Huang Naishu, Liu Peiquan, etc., will also be sent by the Ministry again, and a shareholders meeting is scheduled to be held on the tenth of next month to elect new directors. The general manager will be elected after the board of directors is established.

Personnel of the China Merchants Bureau Debt Reorganization Committee Confirmed 140

Regulations and List to be Submitted to the Ministry for Approval. After the Board of Directors of the China Merchants Bureau resolved to organize a debt reorganization committee, it considered debt reorganization as the only important task at present, and has been actively preparing for it in recent days. As for the regulations of the committee, they have been drafted by committee members Qian Xinzhi and Li Fuxun. The number of reorganization committee members has been decided to be seven. In addition to the four standing directors, Li Fuxun, Qian Xinzhi, Zhang Shouyong, and Ye Zhuotang, who concurrently serve as committee members, lawyers Qin Liankui, accountant Xu Yongzuo, and accounting expert Huang Bingzhang have also been hired as committee members. This was approved by the Board of Directors yesterday, and the regulations and list have been submitted to the Ministry of Communications for review and approval. Once approved by the Ministry, the official establishment will be announced immediately.

Preparing for a Large-Scale Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition 141

Gathering Artists from Across the Country to Support the Northeast Volunteer Army. At this time of year, when the north wind is fierce and pedestrians on the road are wrapped up warmly, if we spare a thought for the three northeastern provinces that have not been recovered, which are still under the enemy's iron heel, and for the volunteer army of patriotic soldiers who are fighting bloody battles in the icy and snowy conditions, hoping to recover the lost territory and revive the dying national spirit, their righteousness and courage should be acknowledged and empathized by people across the country. It is learned that the Shanghai Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association, the China Art Association, and the National Salvation Groups Joint Association have jointly launched a large-scale national calligraphy and painting exhibition to donate all proceeds from ticket sales and various donated calligraphy and paintings to support the volunteer army. Yesterday, the association specially invited famous artists and newspaper reporters in Shanghai to Gongdelin on Parker Road. Those who attended included Di Pingzi, Ma Qizhou, Qian Shoujian, Wu Tianweng, Zhang Yuguang, He Tianjian, Zheng Manqing, Wei Ruosou, Yu Jifan, etc. from the China Art Association, as well as Pan Xulun, Chu Fucheng, Li Cishan, Huang Jingwan, Xie Chengping, Ren Jinping, Hu Zushun, Liu Liumin, Liu Shixiong, Gao Daoyuan, Shen Junru, and newspaper reporters Mi Xingru, Hu Zhuoren, Gu Zhizhong, Xi Xixian, Chen Xiliang, Zhu Yongkang, and other guests, totaling more than eighty people. First, Hu Zushun reported on the preparations and drafted the articles of association, which were unanimously approved and will be established soon. After three rounds of wine, Chu Fucheng, on behalf of the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association and the China National Salvation Groups Joint Association, thanked the guests. The articles of association are recorded below: (Simplified Articles of Association of the National Artists' Aid to the Northeast Volunteer Army Works Exhibition) 1. This association is jointly organized by the Shanghai Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association, the Republic of China National Salvation Groups Joint Association, and the China Art Association, with the aim of raising funds by soliciting works from artists across the country for public exhibition to aid the Northeast Volunteer Army. 2. This association solicits works as follows: A. Calligraphy and paintings by famous people of past dynasties; B. Calligraphy and paintings by famous contemporary people; C. Western painting; D. Sculpture and other art works. There is no limit to the number of works in the preceding items, the more the better. 3. The price of each work is determined by the donor. If it is necessary to recover the cost, please state it in advance, but it shall not exceed three-tenths of the original price. Those who do not state it in advance will be considered as fully donated. 4. This association shall have nine directors, three standing directors, and a number of organizing committee members, who shall be nominated by the three groups and appointed by this association. 5. This association shall have the following groups: 1. General Affairs Group: responsible for handling documents, general affairs, accounting, receipt, dispatch, storage, and matters not belonging to other groups; 2. Propaganda Group: responsible for handling editing, advertising, publishing, and all propaganda matters; 3. Exhibition Group: responsible for handling exhibition venue layout and management; 4. Social Affairs Group: responsible for handling the social and reception matters of this association. 6. Each group of this association shall have one director and a number of staff members, who shall be appointed by the standing directors to handle their respective affairs. 7. The deadline for soliciting works for this association is December 31 of this year. If it is in remote areas, it may be extended to January 15, 1933. The exhibition method and date shall be determined by the standing directors. 8. The receiving addresses of this association are as follows: A. China Art Association, Hualong Road, French Concession, Shanghai; B. Office of the Republic of China National Salvation Groups Joint Association, No. 155 Weihaiwei Road, No. 14, British Concession, Shanghai; C. Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association, No. 29 Ren'an Lane, Guling Road, Shanghai. 9. Matters not covered by these simple articles of association shall be handled by the standing directors through consultation. 10. The preparatory office of this association is located in the office of the Republic of China National Salvation Groups Joint Association, No. 14 Zhongshe, Weihaiwei Road, Shanghai.

Women's Volunteer Army Support Association Launched 142

The wife of Gu Zhutong, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, the wife of Li Jishen, Training Director of the National Government, and the wives of Du Yuesheng and Zhang Xiaolin, directors of the French Concession, deeply concerned about the Northeast Volunteer Army's bloody battles in the icy and snowy conditions, believe that all Chinese people should bear the obligation to provide assistance. Therefore, they have specially launched the Women's Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association, and have taken No. 16 Aveny Court, Avenue Road as the association's location. It is reported that fundraising will begin soon, to provide a strong backing for the Northeast volunteer soldiers.

Donations from Various Places to the Northeast Volunteer Army 143

Yesterday, the Shanghai Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association received a telegram from the Shantou City School Joint Association, reporting that it had remitted 754 yuan through the Bank of China, requesting it to be forwarded to the front lines.

Also, the Fuzhou YMCA remitted 2,000 yuan through the Bank of China, requesting it to be forwarded to the front lines. The Shanghai Postal Workers' Union, considering the Northeast Army's arduous battle to kill the enemy and the need for funds everywhere, launched a fundraising campaign based on the duty of the people to assist. As of the 20th of this month, the members of the union enthusiastically took turns, raising a total of more than 1,200 yuan. It is reported that the union has telegraphed all the donations to the Beijing Postal Union to be transferred to General Zhu Ziqiao and remitted to the Northeast Army for assistance. Donations raised thereafter will reportedly be remitted one after another.

Colleagues from the Salt Affairs Audit General Office launched a monthly donation campaign to support the Northeast Volunteer Army. The first donation was 2,000 yuan, and the second donation was 1,814 yuan, both of which were sent to the Bank of China for transfer to the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association. The third monthly donation of 2,088 yuan was sent through the Bank of China on the 25th of the month. It is reported that the Salt Affairs Audit agencies in various districts have also responded one after another, vowing to be the backing of the Northeast soldiers, in preparation for long-term resistance against Japan.

Communist Party's Top Leader Li Lisan's Wife and Others Transferred to Public Security Bureau 148

The judge ultimately approved the transfer to the Public Concession Police Department. From the 16th of last month to the most recent arrests, thirteen male and female Communist Party members were apprehended. Among them were several key figures, such as Wang Xiuzhen, wife of the Communist Party's top leader Li Lisan, and Chen Binghe and Chen Jincai, both executive committee members of the Communist Youth League. The remaining individuals were also not insignificant. The types of reactionary books seized were too numerous to list. The High Court Second Branch ordered them to be detained separately for further investigation. Yesterday morning was the scheduled trial date. Investigating officers escorted Wang Xiuzhen, Zhang Zhujun, Zheng Xiulan, Wang Li's wife, and four other women, along with Chen Binghe, Chen Jincai, Yang Shifang, Changqing, Zhou Guoxian, He Jinkui, Chen Qiu, Wang Liqing, Zhang Desheng, and nine others, as well as various books and leaflets, to the High Court Second Branch. Judge Yu and assessors Zhao and Guo specially convened a joint court to hear the case. The Municipal Public Security Bureau dispatched officers with an official letter to the court requesting the transfer of all defendants. Attorney Li Zhishan stated that the police department had no objection to the transfer, while several defendants hired attorneys Shi Liang and Deng Jiabing to object to the transfer. A lengthy debate ensued with the Municipal Public Security Bureau's legal counsel, attorney Zhan Jifeng. Ultimately, the court approved the request of the Public Security Bureau's representative attorney and ordered the thirteen men and women, along with the evidence, to be taken back by the Public Security Bureau's officers for further investigation.

Qingchangxiang Foreign Cloth Store

Bomb Thrown Yesterday 149

Two-inch-thick counter board blown into a one-foot hole, all electric lights destroyed, window panes shattered. Qingchangxiang Foreign Cloth Store, located at 463-465 Dama Road, French Concession, corner of Dongxin Street, owned by foreign goods magnate Xu Qingyun (nickname Amao), is a large-scale and highly successful business. At 7:45 PM last night, as the store clerks were resting after dinner, a hand-thrown bomb suddenly flew in from the Dongxin Bridge street side entrance and landed in the center of the counter. An employee happened to be standing next to the counter, initially unaware of what it was. Looking outward, he saw a young man dressed in a patriotic cloth Chinese suit glaring at him. Realizing something was wrong, the employee quickly crouched down behind the counter. About ten seconds later, it exploded with a deafening roar, shaking the surrounding area. The entire room was immediately filled with thick smoke. Nearby detectives arrived upon hearing the explosion. A large hole, about a foot in diameter, was blown into the two-inch-thick counter board. Eight panes of glass were shattered, and all electric lights were destroyed. Fortunately, no one was injured. The detectives collected the remaining bomb fragments and took them to the police station for investigation.

The Tragedy of Difficult Childbirth

Inexperienced Midwife Performed Improper Surgery, Resulting in Mother's Death 150

丨Long Iron Hook Used Over Ten Times丨 丨Fetus Broken and Horrific丨 Chen Haibo, a 41-year-old from Yancheng, lives at 1 Tongxing Street, Lujiazhai, Pudong, where he runs a tea stall. His wife, Li, of the same age, has been working at the British American Tobacco factory sorting leaves for six years. Li has given birth to eight children, five of whom have died, leaving three survivors: a 21-year-old son, a 10-year-old daughter, and a 6-year-old daughter. This year, she became pregnant again. On the morning of the 15th of this month, she suddenly felt abdominal pain, indicating that labor was imminent. Chen hired midwife Xu Zhang (51 years old) to assist with the delivery. After taking her pulse, Xu Zhang stated that the baby would be born by 12:00 PM. However, there was still no sign of delivery at that time. Xu Zhang went to another delivery and did not return until 8:00 PM. Seeing his wife in extreme pain, Chen urgently hired another midwife, Tang Lan (35 years old), from Yangjiazhai. After examining her, Lan stated that it was a difficult delivery and only the mother's life could be saved. She went home to retrieve a long iron hook, about five or six inches long, and other tools. Xu Zhang had also arrived to assist. Lan then began the so-called major surgery, inserting the iron hook into the vagina and using it over ten times to remove the fetus, which was already broken and in a horrific state. Seeing that the surgery was complete, the two midwives tidied up slightly and left. However, two days later, the woman's abdomen suddenly swelled, and her condition became critical. Chen obtained a letter of introduction from the British American Tobacco factory and sent his wife to the orthopedic hospital near Fenglin Bridge in Xuhui for treatment. However, the hospital did not have an obstetrics department and referred her to the Red Cross Hospital. Unfortunately, on the 21st, her condition worsened, and she passed away. Chen had no choice but to take his wife's body back home for burial. He then went to the British American Tobacco factory to claim his wife's life savings to cover the costs of the coffin and burial. However, the factory stated that they required a certificate from the local police station's household registration office before releasing the funds. Upon hearing this, Chen went to the Third District Household Registration Office yesterday morning to register. When officials inquired about the cause of death, Chen told them the truth. The officials stated that the two midwives had not registered with the Health Bureau and did not have licenses. They reported this to the district chief, who dispatched police to bring both women in for questioning. Xu Zhang claimed that she did not perform any procedures, while Tang Lan claimed that she did not use a hook but only reached in with her hand to remove the child and that any marks on the child's body were caused by her fingernails. The district chief, considering that a minor registration issue had led to a loss of life, ordered the two women to be sent to the Public Security Bureau for further action. However, the woman's body, although already in the coffin, had not yet been covered, and the court may be requested to conduct an autopsy.

It's Hard to Be a Wife 153

Husband claims she was not a virgin, requesting doctor's examination three times. Yesterday, a forensic doctor examined her again. The Difficult Life of Tu Fumei.

Song Tianxiang, a doctor from Ningbo, returned to his hometown in October the year before last and married Tu Fumei, a woman from the same village, through a matchmaker. Soon after, he brought her to Shanghai. After living together for a short time, Song suddenly claimed that Tu was not a virgin. Since then, the couple has been at odds. This summer, Tu, feeling unable to live together, hired Lawyer Wu Peng to file for divorce from Song and request alimony. The First Special District Court has repeatedly summoned both parties for questioning, as reported in previous newspapers. The day before yesterday afternoon, Judge Yang conducted the hearing again. The plaintiff's lawyer, Wu Peng, presented a list of dowry items, as the defendant previously stated that Tu had no dowry when she married, proving that the defendant's statement was false. Judge Yang stated that the point of contention in this case was whether the plaintiff was a virgin. He asked if the doctors summoned to testify were present in court. The plaintiff's lawyer stated that they were all present. First, female doctor Zhong Shuzhen testified that although she examined the plaintiff's uterus, she could not be certain, so she told the defendant at the time to ask another doctor to examine her. Then, Dr. Tang Qingyue of Dade Obstetrics and Gynecology Hospital testified that the defendant brought his wife to the hospital to request an examination. He issued a certificate, but he could not definitively prove whether she had given birth or not. Next, Dr. Takayama, a Japanese doctor from Fumin Hospital, testified that on October 25th of the year before last, the defendant and his wife came to the hospital to request an examination of the plaintiff. He confirmed that her hymen was still intact before the marriage and that she had not given birth. However, the defendant claimed to be named Song Wenbin, and the plaintiff claimed to be named Zhang Tu Fumei, saying they were relatives. Then, the plaintiff herself requested that a forensic doctor be sent to examine her again to clarify the truth. The defendant requested that the matchmaker be summoned to testify. Judge Yang adjourned the hearing to summon witnesses for further questioning and ordered Tu Fumei to report to the court at 9:00 a.m. the next morning to await examination by a forensic doctor. Yesterday morning at 9:00 a.m., Tu, following the order, went to the forensic office of the Special Court with her lawyer to request an examination. The doctor had already gone to the forensic examination site on Avenue Petain to examine a corpse. She waited in the lawyer's lounge. The forensic doctor returned to the court at 11:00 a.m. and performed the examination. The results of the examination will be announced at the next court hearing.

The newly appointed Baoshan County Magistrate Jin Qingzhang took office at 1:00 p.m. yesterday. Fishing Organizations Telegram Finance Minister Song Regarding Tax Exemption 155

Telegrams Finance Minister Song regarding tax exemption. Various fishing organizations in Jiangsu and Zhejiang sent repeated telegrams to the National Government regarding the request for tax exemption but received no response. Yesterday, they sent another telegram to Finance Minister Song, stating, "To Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing: The National Government's order of March 28th last year, permanently exempting fish tax and fishery tax, was the utmost expression of President Chiang's and your Excellency's care for fishermen. The fishermen of Jiangsu and Zhejiang were moved to tears. They celebrated the elimination of troublesome taxes and planned to revitalize the fishing industry. However, the economic panic has worsened daily, and fishing villages have declined even more than before. At this time, when they have barely recovered, we suddenly hear that the Ministry of Industry is proposing to reimpose the fish tax. This is detrimental to the government's credibility. Your ministry exempted the tax just over a year ago, and the Ministry of Industry is taking over to collect it. From the perspective of the national tax system, this is also a disruption of the unified system. Our association is determined to unanimously oppose the reimposition of the fish tax. In addition to sending a separate telegram to the Ministry of Industry requesting its cancellation, we earnestly request your Excellency's assistance in requesting the cancellation. The Tax Exemption Maintenance Committee of various fishing organizations in Jiangsu and Zhejiang kowtows."

The Finance Bureau Plans to Standardize the Final Account Methods of Various Agencies 156

Submitted to the Municipal Government for Review and Implementation. The Finance Bureau is currently preparing the final account for 1931 under orders. Recently, the Directorate-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics has issued a temporary charter of final account, with forms and formats slightly different from last year. Therefore, the bureau ordered Dong Zaiqin, an employee of the Budget Division, to carefully plan a method to comply with central regulations and benefit the city's financial administration. Currently, Mr. Dong, based on the shortcomings of various agencies in preparing the final account over the years, and in accordance with the latest regulations and accounting principles of the central government, has drafted 21 articles of the "Unified Method for Preparing the Final Account of 1931 by Various Agencies in Shanghai," as well as various forms, formats, subject classifications, and detailed explanations. They have been submitted to the Municipal Government for review. Once approved by the Municipal Government, they will be issued to various agencies for implementation.

Representatives of Wireless Radio Stations' Clerks Go to Beijing to Petition 157

Requesting the promulgation of regulations and contributing opinions. Xie Chunpu and two others go to Beijing. Since its establishment, the National Federation of Wireless Radio Stations' Clerks has worked tirelessly, making many contributions to the welfare of clerks nationwide. However, radio station clerks generally have specialized knowledge and are mostly hired after examinations, and their work is the same as other service personnel, but their compensation is uniquely different. After the establishment of the federation, petitioning for regulations became the most important work. However, due to the unstable political situation, it has not been filed. Recently, with Yan Renguang as the new Director of the Telecommunications Administration, the federation, in order to implement its original intention, actively urged the matter to be initiated and selected three standing committee members, Xie Chunpu, etc., to go to Beijing to petition. It is also heard that they have attached opinions on improving the wireless communications business for the authorities to adopt. The details are listed below.

Representatives Go to Beijing to Petition. The National Federation of Wireless Radio Stations' Clerks held its twelfth temporary meeting last Friday to discuss the issue of regulations in particular. After investigating the facts in detail, the association drafted 90 articles of regulations and changed the name to Wireless Communications Operators. The association believes that these regulations are of great importance to the welfare of clerks nationwide and has submitted them for serious review again. After they were passed, in order to expedite the promulgation, it was decided to publicly select three standing committee members, Xie Chunpu, Feng Zhenyi, and Shen Yide, to go to Beijing on the overnight train last night and, together with Sha Zongqian, the supervisor of the Nanjing Radio Station General Association, to petition the ministry. It also ordered the Nanjing Radio Station Clerks' Federation to assist in providing proper reception and notified all branch federations of radio stations nationwide.

Reception for the Press Last Night. Last night, guests included reporters from various newspapers, Yu Runsheng, the manager and engineer of the Shanghai General Station, and seven executive committee members of the General Association: Xie Chunpu, Feng Zhenyi, Su Zuqing, Lu Huaiqing, Gu Ermei, Zhang Ruihua, and Shen Yide. After the reception, representatives from the International Radio Stations' Clerks' Association and the Shanghai Radio Stations' Clerks' Association gathered at the General Station at the Old North Gate and departed for the North Station at 10:30 p.m. to send off the representatives to Beijing.

China's Photography Products Strive for Perfection 158

Meeting Situation. At the meeting yesterday, all the committee members attended except for two who were unable to arrive from Beijing and Hangzhou. Song Chunfang, Secretary of the Shanghai Bank, Chen Xiangtao, President of the China Travel Service, Zhang Shuiqi, Committee Member, Hu Shiyuan, Director of the General Affairs Department, and Zhao Junhao, Director of the Publishing Department, provided a warm reception. First, Zhang Shuiqi delivered a speech to report on the progress. Then, Mr. Ye Yufu was publicly elected as chairman, and the following matters were resolved: 1) The originally scheduled collection rules were not perfect and were revised and passed on the spot (the rules are attached). 2) It was resolved to extend the collection deadline to January 10, 1933. 3) It was resolved to invite each committee member to submit a list of must-collect scenic photographs for discussion at the next meeting. 4) It was resolved to ask each committee member to send letters to friends in various places to collect products immediately. 5) It was resolved that the travel agency would invest 1,000 yuan to purchase gifts to be sent to outstanding producers. The detailed method will be discussed at the next meeting. 6) It was resolved that the second meeting would be held at 4:00 p.m. on the 29th of this month (Tuesday) at the Shanghai Bank Library. After the meeting, the travel agency will distribute a copy of "Memories of European Travel" (written by Dr. Chu Minyi), a special book. According to Chen Xiangtao, President of the Travel Agency, the company has always focused on serving the community. Since it has been entrusted by the Chicago Exposition Preparatory Committee, it should solemnly collect various photographs in order to avoid losing national face. In the future, it will also select the best photos, print them in a special book, and use high-quality paper for photogravure printing. The entire book will be explained in English and will be shipped to the United States before the opening of the Chicago Exposition.

Collection Rules (1) This company is entrusted by the product collection office of the Preparatory Committee for China's participation in the Chicago Exposition to collect photographic products. (2) The photographic products to be collected must meet one of the following conditions: 1) Scenic landscapes of various places, 2) Historical sites and antiquities with historical or artistic value, 3) Famous buildings, ancient and modern, 4) Modern new construction projects, 5) Items and customs that can be used for academic reference, 6) Fine art photography works, 7) In addition to the above provisions, excellent works may also be selected. (3) The size of the products to be collected shall be determined by the producer, but the maximum shall not exceed and the minimum shall not be less than. (4) The products to be collected shall be accompanied by detailed descriptions in Chinese and English on separate paper. Those who cannot provide English descriptions may have them translated by the product collection office. (5) The products to be collected shall be carefully sent by registered mail to avoid soiling. It is especially welcome to send the negatives to Shanghai together. If the products or negatives need to be returned, please state in advance. (6) The producers shall provide detailed mailing addresses for communication. (7) If producers in the interior do not have excellent photographers to enlarge the photos, they can send the negatives to this company for enlargement. (8) The products to be collected must be delivered to the Chicago Exposition Photography Products Collection Office, China Travel Service, No. 114 Sichuan Road, Shanghai before January 10, 1933. (9) This company plans to hold a public exhibition in Shanghai in February 1933 for the public to appreciate. (10) When the photography exhibition is held, this company will hire experts to evaluate the products and send the best products to the product collection office of the Preparatory Committee for China's participation in the Chicago Exposition for display in the United States, and this company will send gifts as souvenirs. (11) In addition to the above rules, all other matters concerning the products shall be handled in accordance with the charter of the Preparatory Committee for China's participation in the Chicago Exposition.

Shanghai Northeast Refugee Relief Association 159

Urgent Notice Regarding Monthly Donation Drive. Over a year has passed since the fall of the Northeast. The whole country is silent, relying solely on righteous soldiers who risk their lives and fight bravely. The dead lie in desolate passes, and the living are covered in blood in the icy sky. If we do not expand relief efforts and provide long-term assistance, the righteous soldiers will perish, the Northeast will fall, and China will also perish. Therefore, based on the principle of saving others and saving ourselves, we have publicly discussed the monthly donation method. (1) The monthly donation period is limited to six months. (2) The Northeast Refugee Relief Association in Beiping is the central organization for Northeast relief, presided over by General Zhu Ziqiao. All donations from this association will be remitted for allocation. (3) Operating expenses are borne by the initiators and will not be used for donations. (4) Collection agencies: 1.
