French Liner Arrives in Shanghai 160

Yesterday afternoon, the third new liner of the French Post Shipping Company, Aramis, which departed from Marseille on October 21st for its first voyage to the Far East, arrived in Shanghai and berthed at the China Merchants Bureau North Wharf. The ship is a sister ship to the ill-fated President Doumer, weighing 24,000 tons with tremendous horsepower. The decoration of the first-class cabin is even better than that of Pacific liners. In addition to the dining room, smoking room, gymnasium, swimming pool, etc., a tennis court has also been added. It is the most beautiful new liner on the Central European route. Yesterday afternoon, many people from all walks of life visited the ship. The company sent staff to accompany and entertain the people on board. The maiden voyage back to France is scheduled for three days.

16th Anniversary Celebration of Jisheng Society 161

The Chinese Jisheng Society has been in operation for sixteen years. A grand anniversary celebration was held the day before yesterday. Many people attended. President Huang Hanzhi presided over the meeting. President Xu Qianlin reported briefly that the society was founded on a small scale. Fortunately, due to the efforts of colleagues over the past sixteen years, the society's affairs have developed, and relief funds have been distributed to millions. In the future, we should work even harder. Then, the director of relief affairs reported that the society's relief income this year was far less than in the previous two years, but the relief efforts included winter relief and emergency relief in Wugong, Shaanxi, and running a vocational training center for disaster-stricken children. In Quanqiang, Northern Anhui, emergency relief was provided, and a shelter was set up in Bengbu. Grain was distributed in Guangjiwei, Central Anhui, and seeds were provided in various counties in Southern Anhui, and a loan was provided to Fu Shun Silver Company. A congee factory was established in Gaoyou, Jiangsu, and industrial relief was provided in Jiangning. Emergency relief was provided in Tanghe, Deng County, and Xinye, four counties in Southern Henan, and seeds were also provided in Tanghe and Deng County. The Youren and Liangwei dikes were repaired in Nanchang, Jiangxi, and someone is requesting the construction of Guangfengwei. The Ninghai Dike in Zhejiang and the Zhongdu Bridge in Linhai were reconstructed. The congee factories in Beiping, which had two locations last year, only have one location this year. The amount of medicine distributed this year has more than doubled compared to last year. This year, donations are few and the disaster situation is severe. It is hoped that all those present will contribute generously based on the principle of mutual assistance among compatriots. A certain gentleman reported on the income, expenditure, and academic affairs situation. Mr. Zhu Qichen suggested that the society should print a publication to record in detail the number of donations over the past sixteen years, the relief efforts, and the service of members, so that outsiders can understand the spirit of the society. Everyone agreed. A certain gentleman stated that our country is poor and financially exhausted, but the customs revenue has increased year by year. Up to September of this year, it has exceeded five million taels, which is shocking to hear. In addition, domestic and foreign troubles are on the rise, so that the four classes of people cannot live in peace. Since this society has the purpose of saving the country and saving people, it is clear that in this difficult situation, we must do our best to increase agricultural production to enrich livelihoods and persuade people to save the world. It is not enough to save this calamity.

Songjiang Song Bao Details the Course of Forced Suspension 162

Yesterday, a letter was sent to the press in this city for assistance. The Songjiang Song Bao was ordered to suspend publication by the county party headquarters for publishing news about checking enemy goods. The Songjiang compatriots in Shanghai have telegraphed various parties to appeal. Yesterday, the editor of the newspaper, Shen Shoukang, sent an urgent letter to the newspapers and news agencies in this city, detailing the course of forced suspension and requesting speedy assistance. The original letter is copied below. "We, as a newspaper, maintain a detached position, uphold righteousness, and express public opinion. Since its founding a year ago, the newspaper has unfortunately gained the reputation of society and has been deeply jealous of powerful people. They have used all means to slander and harm us. We have fought alone and endured many hardships. This time, the Songjiang County Party Headquarters believed that the newspaper's publication of the news about checking enemy goods on the 21st of this month was an opportunity that could be used to falsely accuse the newspaper of violating laws and inciting trends, and suddenly sent a secret letter to the county government ordering the Public Security Bureau to suspend publication immediately. At the same time, the police were sent to threaten and monitor the typesetting room. On the 23rd, the newspaper was forced to suspend publication for one day. On the 20th, the incident of checking enemy goods was because Yang and Cai of the Songjiang National Salvation Anti-Japanese Association's party branch checked inferior goods in major silk and cloth shops and had a conflict with the shop assistants of Yuanda Silk and Satin Shop in Shenzhuang Street over the issue of sealing goods. The glass cabinet of the shop was crowded by the audience, and the patrol officer of the second branch of the Public Security Bureau also arrived to suppress the situation. Later, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce mediated. The shop closed its doors afterwards. The location is in a busy thoroughfare, and the incident was witnessed by many people. The newspaper reported based on facts, not on baseless accusations. In addition, all newspapers in Shanghai and Shanghai recorded the incident on the same day. Why was the newspaper the only one to be severely reprimanded? After Yang and others checked the goods, they distributed leaflets everywhere. Why did the county party headquarters not punish them? Is it because Yang and others are employees of the party headquarters and can be propagandists of patriotism? Every citizen is responsible for the rise and fall of the country. The newspaper is responsible for public opinion and dares to be patriotic. The recording of facts is also to fulfill its duty. We did not expect to suffer disaster because of this. Although the newspaper seeks benevolence and obtains benevolence, it is willing to die. However, if this trend continues, it will make the righteous people feel cold. Moreover, according to the regulations on reviewing propaganda, the local party headquarters has no right to punish non-reactionary publications. Since the newspaper has no reactionary propaganda, how can the county party headquarters illegally suppress it to this extreme? Therefore, in order to maintain the solemnity of our press, the newspaper has exhausted its efforts and is not afraid of difficulties. The next day (the 24th), the newspaper was printed and published as usual in another location. The county party headquarters became even more arrogant after learning of this. They sent personnel to order the police to detain the couriers and newspaper vendors, and even the librarians were arrested. Postal deliveries were prohibited, and the station was searched. The situation was so arrogant as if facing a formidable enemy. Under such pressure, the newspaper was unable to continue and was forced to announce its suspension again. This new business in Songjiang is still in its infancy. Once destroyed, the righteousness will decline, and public opinion will be destroyed. The corrupt and inferior people will have no scruples, and the local area will be even more unscrupulous. We have always admired your newspaper for upholding justice. We are especially writing this letter to you to detail the situation. We hope that you will take into account our common culture and provide speedy assistance. The newspaper will be very grateful, and public opinion will be very grateful.

Pickled Meat Industry Continues to Request Exemption from Inspection 164

The Municipal Government Still Rejects. The Pickled Meat and Ham Industry Association of this city previously requested the Municipal Government for exemption from inspection of pickled meat products entering the city, as the Municipal Health Bureau decided to conduct inspections. The Municipal Government has rejected the request. The Municipal Government believes that the inspection of pickled meat products entering the city is for the purpose of maintaining public health for meat consumption. The inspection fee charged is very small and should not have any impact. As for meat products for export to foreign countries, the Health Bureau will notify the central foreign trade commodity inspection agency to send personnel to conduct inspections. Therefore, the request to cancel the inspection is still rejected.

Qiu Changsheng Accused of Conspiring to Seize Inheritance 165

Changsheng did not appear at the initial trial, and reasons were given. Therefore, Qiu Weiqing, a wealthy dye merchant with millions in assets, adopted Changsheng as his son. When dividing the inheritance to his biological young son Changyin and young daughter Shuying, Changsheng, together with outsiders Chang Shuliu and Ren Wei'an, managed and kept a portion of it. Qiu, a fair and just relative of the Qiu family, had long held grievances. Recently, Sun, the second wife of Weiqing, and her younger sister Zhu Qiu, hired three lawyers, Zhang Shizhao, Zheng Wenkai, and Peng Yuanxun, to file a private prosecution against Changsheng and Chang, Ren, in the First Special District Court. At 2 PM the other day, Judge Wu Zhen opened the eighth criminal court to hear the case. The defendant Qiu Changsheng did not appear, and his defense lawyer Wang Fuchang requested a postponement. Chang and Ren hired lawyer Wang Youling to wait in court for questioning. Lawyers Zhang and Zheng both emphasized that Qiu Changsheng was the most important defendant in the case and that his absence without a valid reason was inconsistent with the interrogation methods outlined in Article 41 of the Criminal Procedure Law. The court only inquired about the plaintiffs' intentions for the lawsuit and then adjourned. The remaining proceedings were postponed to the next session. The plaintiffs submitted two indictments. The first indictment jointly sued Changsheng and the other two, while the second indictment focused solely on Changsheng's alleged crimes. The latter indictment is explored and described below:

Respectfully submitting additional facts and reasons, respectfully requesting investigation and verification: It has been found that the defendant Qiu Changsheng has long plotted to seize the inheritance. The facts are as follows, selecting the most obvious points to state: (1) Usurping the name and impersonating a biological son: The defendant was originally the son of the Jiang family, and recently, his biological mother hired a lawyer to send a letter demanding his return to the Jiang clan. When he was adopted by the Zhou family, this was well known by the clan. Therefore, when the genealogy was revised in the past, it was specifically noted that he was an adopted son. The defendant, knowing this was inappropriate, funded a separate publication and attempted to buy back the original genealogy. However, some members of the clan refused to comply. The obituary also clearly indicates that he is not a biological son. This is the first step in the defendant's deliberate scheme to fraudulently obtain the inheritance. (2) The late Qiu Weiqing instructed the plaintiff Qiu Sun to raise his biological children Changyin and Shuying as her own. At the time of his death, he bequeathed Changyin and Shuying to be properly supervised by the plaintiff Qiu Sun. However, knowing that the plaintiff was a woman and that Changsheng was unreliable, he ordered his nephew Qiu Shengshan to manage the property, stating that it could only be returned after the children reached adulthood. This is something the defendant cannot deny. However, the defendant conspired to embezzle the property by sweet-talking the plaintiff Zhu Qiu and the deceased Qiu Jia into jointly suing Qiu Juansan in court, resulting in the actual control being entirely in the hands of the defendant alone. This is the second step in the defendant's deliberate scheme to fraudulently obtain the inheritance. (3) The late husband's inheritance should be inherited by his biological children and the plaintiff Qiu Sun. The defendant, being merely an adopted son, should only receive a small portion of the property. However, he unilaterally divided and obtained as much as 45% of the inheritance. This is contrary to legal principles and human sentiment. Therefore, fair-minded members of the clan, such as clan leader Qiu Hengzhi and nephew Qiu Shengshan, refused to sign the distribution document. The defendant still proceeded with decisive actions to seize the property. This is the third step in his deliberate scheme to fraudulently obtain the inheritance. (4) Qiu Changsheng, being an adopted son, has no maternal affection for the plaintiff. After the late husband's death, he showed no respect for elders and acted arbitrarily. Last winter, the plaintiff, suffering from old age and illness, sought funds from Changsheng to go to Hangzhou for medical treatment to avoid his mistreatment. Changsheng initially refused, but eventually forced her to sign an agreement as a condition. The plaintiff was critically ill and in urgent need of funds, so she had no choice but to comply. Therefore, there was the matter of signing an agreement to separate. For the plaintiff, saving her life took precedence over everything else. For Changsheng, forcing his mother to sign an agreement is unforgivable, even if he is an adopted son. She had labored diligently alongside her late husband for sixty years, resulting in today's fortune. After her husband's death, she was forced to separate by her adopted son. Is there any justice in this world? Furthermore, she earnestly went to Hangzhou for medical treatment, listening to his demands, because Qiu Huang was still alive at the time, and Jia, as the biological mother of Yin, could fulfill her educational responsibilities. She could rest assured that Changyin would be properly cared for. Therefore, she temporarily endured Changsheng's demand to leave home. Now, Jia has passed away, and Qiu Zhou, who adopted Changsheng, has conflicting interests due to her emotional involvement, and she may be biased against Changyin. Now that Jia is dead, Changyin's environment is in danger. The late husband's flesh and blood are only Changyin and daughter Shuying. When Jia was alive, she could not question Jia, but now that Jia is dead, if she does not continue to fulfill her responsibility of nurturing them, how can she face her late husband in the afterlife? This is the reason why she must appeal at this time. The defendant is trying to force the plaintiff to separate in order to achieve his goal of complete control. This is the fourth step in his deliberate scheme to fraudulently obtain the inheritance. (5) After Jia passed away on March 4th this year, the defendant immediately attempted to open the iron safe without permission, which was nearly incomprehensible. The police station was notified, and Detective Chen Yaoting was dispatched to guard the safe for over ten days, preventing him from completely seizing the contents. This is the fifth step in the defendant's deliberate scheme to fraudulently obtain the inheritance. (6) The residence at 184 Tongfu Road has already been allocated to Changyin. However, the defendant still occupies it and refuses to move out, and he has installed iron bars inside the house as if facing an enemy, indicating his clear animosity towards the young boy. This situation can be verified with an inspection. This is the sixth step in his deliberate scheme to fraudulently obtain the inheritance. Based on the above points, the defendant has used various fraudulent tactics to gradually gain control of the inheritance acquired by the plaintiff Qiu Sun during her over twenty years of devoted service to Weiqing. He has also used various threats to eliminate dissent, causing the plaintiff Zhu Qiu, as the closest relative, to fail in her responsibility to protect the young children. There is no doubt that this constitutes a crime under Articles 363 and 365 of the Criminal Law. Therefore, this supplementary explanation is submitted, respectfully requesting the court to investigate and handle the case in accordance with the law. This is truly in the public interest. Respectfully submitted to the First Special District Court of Shanghai.

Suspects Arrested in the Siwen Lane Assassination Case 168

At 2:30 PM the other day, a shooting assassination occurred at 1040 Siwen Lane on Xinzha Road, resulting in the on-the-spot killing of Wang Shouxi (aka Huang Shaoxi) from Yangzhou and wounding Cao Boqian, Wu Xiu, Hao Ming, and Cao's wife, Zhang. The assailants fled. After the incident, the Xinzha Police Station dispatched Chinese and foreign detectives to conduct a thorough investigation, uncovering clues. That evening, around 7 PM, they went to 1151 Gordon Road and arrested Tang Zhang, a 22-year-old woman from Danyang. They then proceeded to 290 Herze Road and arrested Xu Runfeng, a 24-year-old man from Jiujiang. Both were taken to the police station. The following morning, police lawyer Wang Yaotang went to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court and stated that the case was of great importance and that the police were investigating the details and could not disclose them. He requested that the two suspects be detained. Judge Wu Zhen briefly questioned the defendants about their age and hometown and ordered them to be detained for seven days for further investigation. Subsequently, Prosecutor Guo Wei, accompanied by a clerk and a coroner, went to the autopsy site on Feilun Road to examine the body. After the examination, Mr. Guo announced that the deceased Wang Shouxi had died from gunshot wounds inflicted before his death. The body was handed over to Pushan Mountain for burial. The police station was instructed to strictly apprehend the fleeing perpetrators and bring them to justice.

Six Arrested in Songjiang Xingye Bank Robbery Case 169

The Songjiang Xingye Bank robbery case had previously been reported to the provincial government, which approved the issuance of arrest warrants for the robbers to be brought to justice. After receiving a confidential report that the perpetrators were hiding in the French Concession, Lu Ying, the leader of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau's Detective Team, dispatched team leader Chen Guangyan and detectives Zhang Yingpeng to the French Concession to coordinate with Chinese and foreign detectives to investigate the addresses separately. Four men and one woman were arrested. The arrested suspects gave the following statements: (1) Niu Jinpu, 36 years old, from Hefei, Anhui, residing at 6 Meihua Lane, Jupulai Si Road, French Concession, currently the commander of the 3rd platoon of the Special Service Company of the Tax Police Regiment, now stationed in Haizhou. (2) Zheng Shaobo, 27 years old, from Hefei, Anhui, residing at the home of Zhu Guangfu at 2 Denghou Lane, near the Jiuxing Grand Theater, French Concession, formerly a personal guard for Commander Huang of the 88th Division's Independent Brigade. (3) Li Yinghan, 21 years old, from Hefei, Anhui, residing at 7 Dunhou Lane, Julai Da Road, a carpenter. (4) Sun Hanquan, 32 years old, from Hefei, Anhui, residing at 6 Deyuan Lane, Pushi Road, formerly a soldier in the 3rd platoon of the Special Service Company of the Tax Police Regiment. (5) Niu Lang, 32 years old, from Hefei, Anhui, residing at 6 Meihua Lane, Juplai Si Road, married to Niu Jinpu for six years. She stated that her husband was a platoon commander in the Special Service Company and that he took leave to seek medical treatment in Shanghai for an eye ailment. She added, "When my husband was a platoon commander, I worked at a cotton mill in Yangshupu. I do not know what he did outside. Please investigate." (6) Shao, 32 years old, from Chaoxian, Anhui, residing at 6 Deyuan Lane, Pushi Road. She stated, "I used to work as a domestic helper at Niu Jinpu's house. Sun Hanquan often visited Niu's house, so I know Sun. After Niu's wife Lang came to Shanghai, Niu dismissed me and I went to work elsewhere for about two months. Sun Hanquan often visited me, so I quit my job and went to live with Sun Hanquan at Qian Laowu's house. After living there for a long time, it became inconvenient, so Sun Hanquan and I rented a house together in Deyuan Lane. I do not know what Sun did. Please investigate." After verifying the statements, Team Leader Lu was about to proceed when the Songjiang County Government learned of the arrests and sent the captain of the county Public Security Bureau's Detective Team to request the transfer of the suspects for investigation in Songjiang. Team Leader Lu sought instructions from Director Wen, who approved the transfer of the suspects to Songjiang for legal proceedings. It is reported that Songjiang has also apprehended one of the robbers who is currently under interrogation.

Car Driver Bigamy 170

Huang Er girl reported the crime and the driver was sentenced to three years in prison. Zhou Heyi, a 31-year-old car driver from Yangzhou, married Huang Er, a woman from Huaicheng, in Shanghai in 1927. They lived together in a bungalow at 7 Lane 194 Jupulai Si Road, French Concession. This year, in July, Huang Er discovered that Zhou already had a wife, Wu, a woman from his hometown whom he had married in 1921. Wu currently lives in the countryside with Zhou's mother. Huang Er confronted Zhou, but he could not make a decision. On the 4th of this month, Huang Er went to the French police station and accused Zhou of bigamy, requesting his arrest and investigation, stating that she was unwilling to be Zhou's concubine. The police arrested Zhou and brought him to the Second Special District Court, which filed a public prosecution under Article 254 of the Criminal Law. Zhou confessed that his first wife, Wu, had run away and not returned, so he married Huang. He also said that the matchmaker had explained the situation and that he did not understand the law and had not gone through divorce procedures. This spring, Wu suddenly came back and lived with his mother in the countryside. He was now asking relatives to negotiate, allowing him to live with Huang and ignoring Wu. He also hired a lawyer to defend him. The court announced the conclusion of the arguments. Yesterday morning, Judge Wang Gangxu of the First Criminal Court sentenced Zhou Heyi to three years of imprisonment for the crime of bigamy. The defendant remained on his original bail.

Lost Girl Waiting to Be Claimed 174

At 1 AM on the 24th of this month, an unnamed girl, about four years old, got lost in the Great World. She was found by and taken to the police station. The child was wearing a light red fake wool coat and floral Western-style pants, with a hair style , floral shoes, thread socks. She has a towel and a chest pocket on her chest. She could not answer her name or address. The police chief ordered her to be temporarily kept at the police station, awaiting her family to claim her. If any family has lost a child, they can go to the French General Patrol Police Station in Lujiawan to claim her.

The Sixth District Police Station of Caojiadu in West Shanghai yesterday brought back a lost girl, reported to be named Lu A'mei, 14 years old, from Lu Huqiao. She was brought in by a neighbor, stating that she got lost while delivering cloth. Her village is about a dozen miles from Shanghai, so she got lost here. The girl was wearing a striped cloth jacket, had her hair cut short. She is currently being held at the police station awaiting her family to claim her.

Free Talk

Two One Branch Talk

Eating Clams and Growing Beards 177

— Zhan Lu

The Chinese way of relieving boredom is called "[Don't talk about national affairs, eat clams]" This is based on two sentences in the Southern History: "[I don't know what happened, eat clams]" and then changed.

The foreign way of relieving boredom is called "[Don't talk about the recession, grow a beard]" This is a recent anecdote that happened in Nebraska, USA.

Nebraska is a famous prosperous metropolis on the west bank of the Mississippi River, but recently, a cloud of recession has enveloped it. People coming and going in the state are talking about the situation of the recession with furrowed brows. Later, they knew that talking was useless, only adding to the weight of the sadness in everyone's chest. So, the people of the state came up with a way to relieve boredom. All adult men grew beards together. Once they grew a beard, they were tagged with a "[Don't talk about the recession]" sign. Anyone who violates the rule must be fined, and the money from the fine is used as funding for the "[Harvest Festival]" on the 21st and 22nd of last month.

Indeed, with the beard-growing society, many sad atmospheres were eliminated. Everyone stopped talking about the recession and continued to encourage their fighting spirit, restoring the state's past prosperity. If someone asks, "How long will you keep your beard?" they will answer without hesitation, "Until the day prosperity returns." This way of relieving boredom is similar to our country's tradition of "[Don't talk about national affairs, eat clams]" in some ways, but it is also very different in most ways. The recession in the United States is an accidental encounter. It is not known whether this year's recession will turn into prosperity next year. Our national affairs have a trend of getting worse year by year. "[Waiting for the Yellow River to clear, how long will people live?]" If someone asks us, "How long will you eat these clams?" we will also answer without hesitation, "Until the day of peace returns." Then, people will shake their heads in disbelief, or say with a cold laugh, "Hum! Even if you eat clams all your life, you may not have the hope of meeting prosperity again."

Chess Talk 178

— Xu Lianfu

There is an old joke that says, "[Four people, A, B, C, and D, all like to play chess. A and B learned the image of 'a general fighting each other.' As soon as they met, they occupied a room and started playing Chinese chess. C and D, however, disliked the vulgarity of Chinese chess and played the distinct black-and-white Go in the room next to A and B. After a long time, A and B quarreled over the issue of regretting moves, even resorting to violence. But when they heard that the Go friends next door were completely silent, they couldn't help but look at each other and said, 'After all, the gentlemen who play Go have much higher character!' We are all playing chess, but we are making such a fuss. Compared to their quiet and humble attitude, we are truly ashamed.' So, they abandoned the quarrel and decided to go and see C and D's Go. But when they entered the room, they only saw scattered chess pieces, black and white mixed up, and could not find C and D. The two were greatly surprised! Looking around, they found C and D huddled together, crouching in the corner behind the wall, unresponsive when called and unmoved when pushed. Touching their bodies, they were both stiff and icy, and they had died! It turned out that they fought to the death because of mutual fights, and they fought until C strangled D's throat against the wall and D grabbed C's testicles. The two of them became a dead end!"

The more high-ranking and respected gentlemen are, the more likely they are to fight to the death! It is a pity that this chaotic situation is even more hopeless to resolve!

New Seedlings 179

— Jiuzhi

In recent years, the morals of the world have been declining, and the tricks of deception at sea are becoming more and more bizarre. My younger brother told me that the other day, because of illness, he went to Huang Yizhao, a one-finger Zen massage doctor, for treatment. He heard someone outside the window at the registration desk asking for a doctor. Huang said, "Today, another person is trying to use counterfeit money!" He hurried out and, after a while, returned to the examination room. My younger brother asked how he knew someone was using counterfeit money. Huang said, "I heard something strange in his words. He claimed to live on Route Lafayette and, because his father was ill, he was introduced by the Zhang residence on the same road to invite me for a consultation. This is normal. What's strange is that he said he came from Route Lafayette, but his direction was from south to north. My house is located on South Chengdu Road near Changbang Road, and it's the first house at the entrance of Alley 21. It's easy to find when looking from south to north, but he said he went straight to North Chengdu Road before turning back here. Considering the circumstances, I suspected him, so I investigated. According to the registration desk, he initially presented two ten-yuan bills, asked to get a number for a consultation, and asked for a change of seven yuan and two jiao. Then, he registered for an outpatient number, took back one ten-yuan bill, and asked for a change of seven yuan and ten jiao. Moreover, he said that his father's illness was the same as Mr. Zhang's. Mr. Zhang's chronic illness is very serious, and he has been treated by me for many days but still cannot leave the house. Yet, this person suddenly wanted to get a number and come here for treatment. Considering the illness, I found it contradictory, so I knew he was using counterfeit money. Fortunately, the person registering at my house was alert and, seeing his panicked appearance, didn't want to repeat yesterday's mistake. So, he held the bill he presented, intending to exchange it at a tobacco and paper store. Seeing that his plan wouldn't work, he quickly snatched the bill and left." My younger brother was speechless with amazement after hearing this.

Remembering the Qing Daoist 180

| Postscript to the Lost Manuscripts of Jiang Sishi Yu'an Meihua'an | Li Meihua'an of Linchuan, my teacher, has passed away for twelve years. Many of his lost manuscripts were occasionally seen in the margins of books and in letters. Hu Guangwei Xiaoshi, a fellow student, invited the teacher's son, Zhongqian, in the second month of the year Jiazi, and gathered at Mr. Nongran's studio. They held the teacher's lost writings, like when he jokingly signed "The Complete Book of Everything," totaling seventeen volumes. They copied and compiled six volumes and sent them to the Sanyuan Jingshe, while entrusting the remaining writings to Zhongqian. Among all his sons, the teacher loved Zhongqian the most. He personally taught him, and Zhongqian inherited his calligraphic skills, able to establish himself. After the fifteenth of that month, Bang and Yinshuang concluded at the Youmei Hall on the lake. Mr. Sanyuan built a congratulatory green cottage, showed the copy, and returned it. Due to his aging mood, he didn't bother to manage it. Later, he finally obtained his preface. Bang carefully examined the teacher's lost writings, finding many errors or incompleteness, with some parts drafted by his students. Correspondence with friends, like chronological arrangements, could not be known without someone as intimate and loving as Zhongqian. However, Zhongqian was slow and procrastinating. Although Bang urged him, he couldn't complete it for years. In the small spring of the year Bingyin, Zhongqian went far to Nanyang, and news of him ceased. Some even said he was no longer in this world. Alas, will the teacher's lost writings ultimately remain sealed in a worn-out box, their voice and glory hidden as if they never existed? Bang's learning is rough and fragmented, and he dared not take on the heavy task. Knowing that changes require thorough investigation, he consulted with fellow students Zhang Shanzi Daqian and Jiang Wanping Zhu Dake, urging Xiaoshi again, but without response. Turning to strict supervision of Bang, he reluctantly took what was compiled, categorized, and chronologically arranged, along with what he knew, and divided the lost writings into several volumes. He also divided the years of compiled manuscripts into several volumes of lost drafts. The seventeen volumes of lost ink that Zhongqian took were also found after much searching, but they were fragmented and scattered, with multiple hands, and messy scribbles, making them impossible to compile. Working day and night, he sifted through them, making a collection of lost ink and writings. At the end, he attached the teacher's remarks on his fiftieth birthday and eulogies, asking his friend Yiping Zhai to finalize them. After completion, the fellow students planned to publish them. Alas! The teacher's noble character and integrity were such that, after the national upheaval, even children and vendors knew of the Qing Daoist. His solitary indignation was expressed in his writings, and the world should understand his suffering. His calligraphy integrated the North and South, blending steles and rubbings, imitating the Tang and Song, following the Six Dynasties, tracing back to the Qin and Han, and leading back to the Three Dynasties. Freed from stone, he sought from tripods and platters, Yuzhao's Dragon Gate, and Kongmen's calligraphy. The teacher should have been an expert, but unfortunately he passed away early and had no monographs. A scale and a claw are only occasionally seen in Lu Shi's script in Zhonglang Zi'an's collection. With no Baishi in the world, who can continue Guo Ting's calligraphy manual? Therefore, the teacher's legacy should be even more cherished than the theories established by recent scholars Ruan and Bao. Mr. Nongran initially held the teacher's teachings, but it was not here, and Zhongqian secretly held his strength. He knew that scholars would still rely on this for exposure. It is painful that the teacher sold his calligraphy for a living, a deep hidden pain. Having failed to adorn him with a yellow crown and invite a posthumous title, his resentment lies buried in the spring. If this culture is not extinguished, perhaps it will also fulfill the teacher's legacy? It is also touching that Zhongqian, with his early reputation like a bright pearl, and deep love like a copper plate, fully prepared for kindness and grace, should have persevered, but ultimately ended up in a foreign land, entrusting this heavy burden. It is only entrusted to someone like Guo Bang, who has no skill or art to inherit his virtue. In a year when foreign enemies are invading, he is undertaking the task of investigating star notes, worrying about the sky and pointing to the sun, guarding the gate and remaining doubtful. This compilation is worthless. Alas! Eight-brick broken inkstone, a scroll of spring clouds, tears dripping on the Yellow Dragon, spirits saddened at Niu Shou (the teacher's collection of Ruan's Eight-Brick Inkstone and Gao Fangshan's Spring Clouds at Dawn scroll both belong to my studio), caressing relics is also a self-redemption. Xiaoshi initiated the compilation, and the Jiang and Zhang disciples facilitated it later. The teacher's disciples are sincere, and their friendship is unmatched. As for the diligence of copying and interviewing, Zhong Jun Dehan's son Xiqin also worked hard. Winter Solstice, year Xinwei.

The Crossroads of Death (226) 181

— Fan Yanqiao

It came, the elevator came. Gengsheng let the woman step in first, following closely behind. A briefcase accidentally bumped her right arm. She recoiled her right arm, cast a glance at Gengsheng, followed by an extremely slight, extremely faint smile. This smile added even more to Gengsheng's suspicions. Although she was being reserved for the sake of her red lips, the two shallow dimples on her rosy cheeks clearly revealed Ai Gu's characteristics. The elevator reached the ground floor. Chi let her go first. He followed behind, seeing her slip into a white-plated car and whirring away. He let go of all his fantasies and went to do his official business.

That evening, he went to the Southeast Hotel to find the company commander again. It was already past twelve o'clock. The elevator was extremely crowded with passengers. He was forced into a corner of the elevator by a woman who squeezed in from the second floor, making it difficult to even breathe. Finally, he heard the elevator operator say, "Fourth floor!" He pushed through the crowd and walked out. Hey! He met the woman again. The one who came in on the ground floor didn't have this woman. This woman must have been the one who squeezed in on the second floor, making it difficult for me to breathe. Walk over. Turning back to look, it was even stranger. It was the woman he suspected to be Ai Gu during the day. At this point, he couldn't help but be a little careful. He deliberately walked slower, letting the woman walk ahead, and then followed. He turned a corner and stopped in front of room 436. The room attendant came to open the door, and she walked in. With a bang, the door closed.

After he met with the company commander and finished his official business, he came out and walked past 436, seeing the door still closed. The nameplate on the door read "Jiang." He was discouraged. But when he reached the ground floor, his dead heart rekindled. He asked the cashier, "What kind of person lives in room four hundred and thirty-six?" The cashier, seeing that he was wearing a military uniform, a armed belt, and carrying a briefcase, did not dare to be slow and had a somewhat flattering attitude. He went to flip through the guest register and came back to say, "She's been here for a month. She seems to be from Suzhou. I don't know what she does. If you want to find out, ask the room attendant." At this time, a very young man next to him interjected, "Four hundred and thirty-six?" He smiled and said, "A dancer from the Neon Dance Hall." Gengsheng didn't ask any further. Instead, the cashier minded his own business and asked the young man, "How do you know?"

"Don't you read the tabloids? Who doesn't know the famous Jiang Aili?"

"I'm ashamed. How could I not notice this bright and shining dancing star, constantly flashing before my eyes?"

"I even saw a secret history of her published in a Shanghai tabloid, saying that she was a concubine who was divorced from a wealthy family in Suzhou. Recently, she was also taken by a Suzhou refugee, who will probably return to Suzhou to be his concubine."

"Hmph! ...... Women these days are really carefree. Today, they are happy to cohabitate with you. Tomorrow, they are unhappy and take my clear autumn road." "That's not entirely the women's fault. In many cases, it's really the men's fault."

"..............."

The young man leaned closer and whispered to the cashier, "Four hundred and thirty-six is here."

Gengsheng didn't have anything else to ask. He walked out of the cashier's room and came face to face with the woman. The woman looked at him, but stopped. Gengsheng looked at her and also stopped. Even the people walking in and out stopped. Gengsheng was the first to feel embarrassed and turned to leave. The woman suddenly caught up and asked, "May I ask your esteemed name?"

This abrupt question was naturally very tense. He replied, "My surname is Liu," while reviewing her from head to toe again, and then calmly responded.

"Where is your home?"

"A village in the countryside of Suzhou."

"What is the name of the place?"

"Cuiwei Village."

"Hmm! ......" She was so anxious that she almost shouted it out. She calmed herself down and looked at Gengsheng again, especially paying attention to the number cloth on his chest. Gengsheng also felt it, so he simply told her everything, saving himself from constantly holding it in. Perhaps after saying it, there would be new developments. ...... Sure enough, the woman heard him say that his name was Liu Gengsheng, guessing that she disliked the name A'gen and changed it. It was the same as her changing her name to Jiang Aili. At this point, there was no need to be suspicious. It must be him. So, she said, "I am Ai Gu. Do you have something to talk about? Would you like to come to my room to discuss it in detail?"

(Soaring by over 13 Taels) Yesterday, the upward trend intensified, rapidly advancing with few setbacks. This Month's Bonds Auction Has Been Stopped 187

| Only the December Term is Open, Market is Still Prosperous | | Prices are Firm and Rose by 0.7-0.8 Jiao Compared to Before | Yesterday (26th), the Shanghai Chinese Securities Exchange stopped trading in the November futures of bonds in advance to facilitate the handling of various procedures before the settlement of the next Tuesday. The January 1922 futures will be opened for auction from today. Yesterday, there was only one type of market in December. The cash ins and outs were only 22,000 yuan. As for the prices of various bonds, although this month's auction has stopped, it is close to settlement, but the market sentiment is still good. Both are the highest prices this year. Other bonds have also increased by about 0.6-0.7 jiao.

Yarn and Flowers

The Quiet Yarn Market 189

丨The Last Transaction of Yarn This Month Dropped Five Cents丨

The cotton yarn market has entered a quiet and lifeless state, but the trend is still softening. The actual demand in the market is quite sluggish, and all parties show no enthusiasm. The end of the year is approaching rapidly, and funds are becoming tighter, so most people are bearish. Today is the last day of this month. The short sellers slightly reduced their positions and hedged into other months, so the situation remained calm. However, in the last transaction, the sellers were extremely strong, resulting in a drop of five cents, to 138.5 taels, with a total transaction volume of approximately 4,000 bales.

(People's Standard Stagnation) The People's Standard market opened lower, influenced by the downward trend of American cotton. Trading in the market was light, and selling pressure was not strong. Due to the increase in gold prices, prices for all months rose by two, three, four, and six cents. In the afternoon, the current month fell by nine cents, while distant months rose by one cent. The total transaction volume for the day was 28,700 bales. The transaction volume for the previous month was 17,000 bales. Shipments included 1,100 bales from Zilai, 750 bales from Shenji, 650 bales from Yiyu, and 450 bales from Xincheng. Purchases included 950 bales from Jifeng, 850 bales from Yukang, 750 bales from Renfeng, 500 bales from Gengfeng, and 550 bales from Dafeng. The closing prices are listed below:

The Cotton Market Shows a Slight Upward Trend 190

丨Stocks Appear Too Scarce丨

American cotton has been trending downward for days, and spot prices have also broken the six-cent mark. However, due to the surge in gold prices and the depreciation of exchange rates, prices have risen in effect, if not in appearance. Therefore, the market not only has not fallen, but has tended to rise. The main reason is the lack of arrivals from all sources and the weakness of inventories. Therefore, the yarn market is sluggish and the environment is deteriorating. All these situations are viewed pessimistically. However, the stocks of local cotton are too small. The delivery volume in November was less than 10,000 dan. Although foreign cotton prices are cheap, they are difficult to import to Shanghai due to the influence of exchange rates. As a result, even if some manufacturers try to sell off, there is no room for prices to fall in the near future.

(Zheng Standard Near Good by Two Cents) The Zheng Standard market opened higher. Due to the rise in gold prices, even though American cotton fell, the calculated silver price was still high, so there was a lack of new sellers in the market. Prices for all months rose by five cents to one cent. In the afternoon, prices rose again by five cents to one cent. The total transaction volume for the day was 36,000 dan, compared to 64,000 dan on the previous day. Shipments included 4,100 dan from Shenchang, 2,800 dan from Yuanxingchang, 1,300 dan from Mingde, and 4,400 dan from Rongxing. Purchases included 1,900 dan from Changfeng, 1,000 dan from Yifeng, and 1,000 dan from Tongxing. US Cotton Restricted by War Debt Issues 193

New York, November 25th dispatch: This week, the cotton market in the South slightly sold off, but it was mostly offset by purchases from fellow traders. General transactions were restricted due to the lack of progress on war debt issues. Most December futures positions were closed out before the date of delivery notices, and distant month positions were also closed out from time to time, resulting in a price easing. Only a small amount of buying interest occurred when prices fell, and merchants appeared willing to wait for further developments in the spot market in the South or the general situation. It is reported that Japanese traders have purchased raw cotton at low prices, and European traders have recently purchased a small amount. Reports estimating a decrease of 200,000 bales in Chinese cotton production and news of the Egyptian government restricting cotton fields next year have had no significant impact on the New York market.

Grain and Rice Market Trends Turn Downward 194

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, about thirty to forty ships from various parties arrived. Sales on this street were smooth, and there were some scattered transactions. The market for thin rice and early rice was poor, except for short-sized Changxi Beigeng and Sutong Baigeng. Ban Yang Dujian arrived and sold evenly. The market showed no upward or downward movement.

(Xinzha) Although there were few arrivals yesterday, there are about 250 accumulated boats of riverside dealers, each with about 80 shi, totaling about 20,000 dan of goods. The market opened in the morning with a general drop of one jiao for thick geng, early thin rice. However, the Bianyin Yuan wine dealers had some dealings, and the market stabilized. The Lupu Jian had no interest at all from downstream.

Customer Xian Min Sales Continue Strong 195

Yesterday, the foreign rice market was nonexistent and still in a state of stagnation. There were continued arrivals of Hunan and Jiangxi customer xian, totaling 3,000 bags. However, the customer xian business was very active in Fujian, with Quanzhou and the provincial capital showing great interest. However, fearing a sharp rise in prices, they did not fully load. Yesterday, Quanzhou had a stronger interest than the provincial capital, which yielded to Quanzhou. Quanzhou originally planned to take over more than 200,000 bags designated for the disaster area in southern Fujian, with Jinjiang County alone accounting for more than 50,000 bags, and other places accounting for 20,000, 30,000, or 50,000 bags. Currently, only one-tenth or two-tenths has been loaded. It is expected that there will be a huge amount of consumption in the future. The provincial capital has even greater interest, and there is a military demand. Therefore, the market will continue to be smooth and orderly in the future. If the market becomes too large, it may be necessary to change to other ports for inquiry. Yesterday, the general market opened with 2,500 bags of Hunan machine oil rice at 8 yuan, 8 jiao, 2 fen, and 8 yuan, 7 jiao, followed by 8 yuan, 5 jiao. There were also 380 bags of Machine Jinggang rice at 8 yuan, 3 jiao. There were also 300 bags of Jing rice at 7 yuan, 2 jiao and a half to 2 jiao. There were also 70 bags of Machine Mi rice at 8 yuan. Anqi coarse Yuan rice had a new arrival yesterday and sold 250 bags at 6 yuan, 3 jiao to 6 yuan, 1 jiao. In addition to the local Beibang, which took 200-300 bags, Fuzhou took 400 bags, and the rest were all taken by Quanzhou.

The Starch Market Shows Stable Trend Following Factory 196

Yesterday, after the opening in the morning and afternoon, the starch market generally showed stability. Foreign wheat quotations fluctuated slightly. However, most manufacturers were still hesitant to sell, and general short sellers had little to do because of the low exchange rate and the near absence of Australian wheat quotations. Therefore, short sellers had some covering. The current month was still affected by spot conditions, and Hwafung had covering in all transactions. December had a slight sale. Distant months saw the market rising gradually due to the persistent support of large factories. Future rises and falls will depend on the state of the factories. As a result, the current month rose by 2.5 li compared to the previous day, December rose by 7.5 li, January rose by 2.5 li, February, March, and April rose by 1 fen, and April rose by 7.5 li.

The Wheat Futures Market Is Relatively Lively 197

亅Many Long and Short Positions Closed Out in This Month丨

Yesterday, after the market opened in the morning and afternoon, the wheat futures market showed a slight vitality, and trading was also slightly smoother. As the current month was the last day, many long and short positions were closed out. The opening price in the morning was 3 qian 5 fen, then down a little bit. The market generally revolved around December to January in the afternoon with little trading and no change in the market. Trading in March and April was smooth. The market rose slightly due to the continued rise in the gold market. As a result, the current month was slightly lower by 1 fen compared to the previous day, March was better by 1 fen, April was better by 2 fen, and there was no change in the rest.

Silk Tea India Increases Import Tax 199

Rough Silk Sales to India Become Difficult

Since the Indian government implemented an increased import tax on raw silk, the cost of shipping Chinese silk to India has increased. Indian merchants in Shanghai are reluctant to buy yellow and white rough silk due to the high prices, and imports have decreased. Since the new silk came on the market this year, Indian merchants have purchased less than 50% of the amount of yellow and white rough silk compared to previous years. The number of Chinese silk shipments to India on ships to England has been decreasing. The sales of rough silk to India are unlikely to improve in the short term due to the high tax.

The Depression Slightly Moves The Precious Eyebrows' Sales 200

The precious eyebrow green tea from Wuyuan and Tunxi has recently seen a slight increase in sales to Europe due to the repeated price drops in tea. British merchants such as Yihe, Xiehe, Jinlong, and Tongyun have had telegram transactions almost daily, with a total transaction volume of no less than 1,200 boxes. Most merchants have also sent out large numbers of telegrams, and the market is slightly more active than before. However, Wubei precious eyebrow has fallen to over 80 taels, Tunxi Wudong goods have fallen to 60-70 taels, Xixian Weiping goods have fallen to 50 taels, and Wenzhou Tuzhuang goods have fallen to 30-40 taels. Chinese tea merchants have suffered exceptionally large losses.

The Sugar Market Coarse Sand White City Trend Rises Again 201

丨丨丨 But No Transaction丨丨丨

Yesterday, the sugar market saw a further rise in the gold price and repeated shrinkage in the Dutch exchange rate. The official price set by the association boosted confidence. No. 24 coarse sand white [unclear] was priced at 15.5 taels, and ordinary goods were priced at 15.3 taels. However, because the actual sales were weak, no transactions took place. However, with the cost of capital increasing, it seems difficult to suppress the market in the future. A new shipment of Qing brand was continuously transported by Yihuo Company Hengsheng ships totaling more than 700 bags. Because the market was weak, only a hundred or so bags were sold, and the price fell to 8 taels and 9 qian. Today is a Sunday and there is no market for other goods.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Essay

Resistance 218

— A Sheep

Everyone says... [the Chinese people have little resistance]. Judging from the September 18th Incident, this may be true to some extent, but the facts cannot be completely ignored. It should be known that resistance exists where it is possible. Let us not talk about the spirit of resistance of the 19th Route Army and the Northeast Volunteers who have suffered for a year, but just talk about recent events in our country, which are enough to prove the general resistance of the Chinese people.

First, there was the dispute between the two Chens in Guangdong, with the magnificent spirit of mutual resistance, such as airplanes sinking the Feiying warship. Then, there was the recently resolved battle between Han and Liu in Shandong, with thousands of cannons fired in a single day and the resolute spirit of attacking and defending to the death. In addition, there is the ongoing conflict between the two Lius in Sichuan. These can all be regarded as outstanding examples of resistance.

Putting aside the resistance of national soldiers (?), let's look at the resistance of the people. There are plenty of examples here...

Wasn't the economic boycott a big deal after September 18th? Then there was the January 28th Incident, which further aroused people's emotions. During this period, the economic boycott did have a good effect. However, after the agreement was signed, some people secretly engaged in trade, which slightly revealed their ability to resist. Therefore, patriotic groups issued warnings. Although they were formally hidden, they were still very active underneath, which is a further manifestation of resistance. And now? The power of patriotic groups seems insufficient to deter them. They simply shout and yell and engage in trade, further invigorating their resistance. Don't you see news in the newspapers these days about "[inferior goods entering in large quantities]," "[goods arriving in crowds]," and "[Japanese shipping resuming]"? Serious national crisis is not enough to awaken their conscience, and the warnings of patriotic comrades cannot deter them. The indomitable spirit of selling my goods and buying my goods is not a full expression of resistance?!

Apart from this, let's talk about a corner of society. What about the resistance there?

In places where urination is prohibited, no matter how strict the warning is, "[those who violate will be sent to the authorities and severely punished without leniency]," and even drawing turtles or using the most extreme curses, people still urinate disrespectfully and recklessly. After putting up sputum containers and writing "no spitting," the sputum containers become decorations, and people spit everywhere. All these indicate the resistance of the Chinese people.

Huh! Who says the Chinese people have no resistance?

Literature and Art

Presented to Liu Shou Die 219

— Wu Tiansheng

Each has their own poverty and sorrow, and refuses to rest. Together, we face urgent difficulties in the ancient southern state. Who understands the broken family and pities the chickens and dogs? In the end, the road leads to bearing the burden of horses and cattle. It's hard to know whether to cry or laugh, gazing at each other silently. Throughout the ages, it's a lonely sight. There's nothing left to do in this world, so let a bit of green mountain pierce the white head.

Feelings on Current Events 220

— Mo Ke

Looking at my reflection in the mirror, I sigh, "Alas!" Whose help can I rely on in this declining world? Showing love for talent only leads to axes that chop branches. Bringing food still startles the crows that feed their parents. The west wind sweeps across the land, drying up the bones of ten thousand people. The fires of Qin cover the sky, restoring the practices of the scholars. If Heaven's will and human affairs are truly like this, then let's drink a hundred jugs of Qingzhou wine.

Science

Alum 221

— Gu Lvshuang

Alum is a general term for a class of compounds, a double salt composed of one part metal sulfate and one part trivalent metal sulfate. Because of the different components, there are potassium aluminum alum, ammonium aluminum alum, potassium chromium alum, and so on. The alum we ordinary people refer to is potassium aluminum alum, which contains one molecule of potassium sulfate, one molecule of aluminum sulfate, and twenty-four molecules of water. This article refers specifically to this common alum. This substance is extracted from a mineral called alunite. The alunite is heated, and the soluble part is extracted with water to obtain alum crystals. The largest producers in the world are Rome and Hungary.

Alum is used for water purification, not only in mainland households, but also in water plants in large cities, where it is used as the first step in the water purification process. Please first describe the chemical principle of its water purification, which is also a common knowledge.

The composition of alum is as described above. Among them, aluminum sulfate, after entering the water, encounters the inherent carbonic acid or carbonates in the water, and is transformed into aluminum bicarbonate. This substance is hydrolyzed to form aluminum hydroxide, and the water purification effect is based on the formation of the latter.

When aluminum hydroxide is formed, it first becomes a colloid, suspended on the water surface, and gradually forms a colloidal precipitate. When this precipitate settles, it carries away all the fine particles in the water, such as bacteria and mud particles, and the water becomes clean. However, bacteria cannot be completely removed, so water purified with alum cannot be drunk raw and must be boiled again. This is something we often misunderstand, and unknowingly suffer from.

In medicine, alum is used as an astringent and has a wide range of uses. In the past, it was also used internally to stop diarrhea and bleeding. Today, it is mostly used externally. The most common use is as a gargle with a 0.5% to 1% aqueous solution, which is very effective for tonsillitis (commonly known as enlarged tonsils). Or, the powder can be blown into the nose and throat to treat inflammation of the nose and throat. There is some reason for rural folk to sprinkle the powder on rotten sores on the hands and feet. Also, alum mixed with vinegar has a disinfecting and swelling-reducing effect and can remove all nameless swellings.

There are many types of fermentation powder, all of which are made by combining baking soda and a substance that causes the baking soda to release carbon dioxide. Alum can also be combined with baking soda to make a fermentation powder, called alum fermentation powder. Its chemical action is too complex to be discussed here.

This substance can also be used to make fireproof cloth. Its crystals attached to the fabric are easily dissolved, and this dissolved substance can prevent the fibers from coming into contact with air, thus having a fire-resistant effect.

The aluminum acetate solution obtained by the reaction of alum and acetic acid can be used to make waterproof cloth. The method is to immerse the cloth in this solution and then put it in a steam box, where the aluminum acetate hydrolyzes to produce aluminum hydroxide. This substance attaches to the pores of the fibers, making them water-repellent.

Alum is something we regard as worthless, but who knows that this worthless thing has such great uses? Therefore, I have listed a few to provide for the readers of this publication.

Sketches of Student Life 222

— Wen Bing

I have been away from student life for a whole year. Sometimes it makes me nostalgic with memories! Sometimes it makes me curse and scold! Who doesn't say that... student life is everyone's golden age. A rosy, comfortable life/Yes. Absolutely right, but unfortunately, most people have drifted through it in a dream. At least, that's how I feel. And repent! Friends, this is not me intentionally slandering our own people!

To be romantic is to be a notable figure. So, when snowflakes are flying and wind and rain are raging, wearing only a thin, long gown and dragging on slippers, or even enslaved Guangdong wooden clogs, with a hat tilted sideways, shivering and pacing into the classroom is the style of a scholar. This attracts attention and makes female classmates smile. Sometimes the clothes are indeed beautiful, but the dirty clothes that have been taken off are too lazy to ask the servant to wash. One by one, they are stuffed under the bed. Over time, the filth fills the dormitory and makes people sick. After paying for meals, sometimes I don't feel like eating my fill. Anyway, when my stomach is hungry, there are plenty of restaurants at the door selling fried noodles, wontons, and noodle soup, which are all quite filling. One or two bowls fill the stomach, the account is written in the book, and with books in hand, I turn around and skip away. This also provides extra income for many vendors.

Saying that modern students don't work hard is a bit unfair! When going to the toilet, which student squatting on the toilet doesn't hold a book in their hand and read diligently? When attending a memorial week or listening to a scholar's lecture, who doesn't carry a book, listening to the lecture while reading their book, or even placing a book on the table while eating? Aren't these manifestations of hard work? Heaven knows!

It is natural to boycott bad teachers. But in fact, the degree of a teacher is not the only standard for boycotting. If a teacher is too strict, doesn't allow leniency in exams, or forbids reading love letters and flirting in class, then he should be careful. Students will not only say that he has poor eloquence, but will also criticize the lecture notes he compiled for being incomprehensible, and even slander his character! Hooking up with female classmates is even worse. You can only roll up your bedding and run away. It's truly a wrong! When there is turmoil in the school or chaos in the country, everyone is extremely happy. Emotions rush in, reason is thrown aside, and there is a blind commotion. An anonymous leaflet is posted. Anyway, there is plenty of free time, and some take advantage of this free time to snuggle in the arms of their lovers. Donating to the Northeast Volunteer Army? Performing plays to raise money for disaster relief? That is just a convenient add-on. Why bother being so busy? The school's schedule can be changed at will. The sun is high in the sky, and it's time for class, but I'm still snoring in bed. After the lights go out at night, I light a candle. When the training director comes to check, I cover it with paper. When asked why I'm doing this day and night, I'll give a whole set of reasons. The only purpose of entering school is naturally to attend classes and listen to lectures to gain some knowledge for life. But in fact, most students don't like to attend classes. Being late and leaving early is still a good phenomenon. Some simply run away after roll call, and some simply ask someone to represent them. When the exam is approaching, being able to cram the night before is still a good phenomenon. Some are still snuggling with their lovers in the girls' dormitory or indulging in the cinema. Fortunately, during the exam, not only can you [cheat], but the teachers are also understanding and provide detailed explanations and hint at flipping through books.

This seems too harsh, but I feel that these are just a few outstanding examples. Try to open our eyes and see. Isn't the reality displayed like this? I can't help but put down my pen and sigh again.

Disappearance 223

— Yi Ping

Before dawn, the dew soaks the ankles. Farmers working in the fields can no longer linger in warm beds. They get up early to prepare their farm tools and go to the fields. Even Sister Zhao, who herds ducks, carries a willow branch and follows behind a flock of ducks, singing mountain songs like "Private Love" while skipping and running.

Sister Zhao was already sixteen years old when spring came. She drives the ducks out every morning and drives them back in the evening. Her daily life is like this. She knows no sorrow or worry. The ducks enjoy the water in the river, and she lies on the grass by the riverbank, looking at the blue sky and watching the white clouds, imagining whatever she wants. Sometimes she plays chess with the cowherd riding on the ox, wading through the water. She does everything and does it willfully.

But today, a special emotion has arisen in our Sister Zhao. She drags the willow branch and is too lazy to follow the ducks. The spring breeze blows her temples, and she seems to shake her head without paying attention. She is completely calculating the words that Lin Sheng, the young master of the duck's home, said to her. She inadvertently misses a riverbank and casually drives the ducks down to the river beach. She secretly takes out a book that Lin Sheng stuffed into her small pocket. The cover depicts a beautiful princess. She reads a few pages, understanding but not fully understanding. It seems like a prince is proposing to a princess, etc. It is somewhat similar to what Lin Sheng said to her. Suddenly, two red clouds fly onto the tips of her cheeks. She leans over and sees her reflection in the river. She is indeed as beautiful as a princess [Lin Sheng's words are correct, I don't look like a villager].

She thinks that the sky seems to be transforming into a bustling city, like the Shanghai she dreams of. Lin Sheng said that Shanghai has cars, electric lights, and beautiful women. Since Lin Sheng loves me, I will go to Shanghai with him. He will not deceive me. Thinking of this, she is embarrassed to think further. The joy and fear that a mature virgin should have are intertwined with a self-conscious smile.

Suddenly, her eyes are covered by a hand reaching from behind. She feels insulted and curses, "Ah Gou!" Ah Gou, who plays chess with her every day, didn't expect Sister Zhao to scold him today, and walks away dejectedly. Sister Zhao's inexplicable feelings win out in her heart. After a long, long time, Sister Zhao drives the ducks back home. The master, Liu Laosan, says gently, "Sister Zhao, you've worked hard." Hearing this sentence that she is used to hearing every day, Sister Zhao feels today as if Liu Laosan is hiding another meaning. She sees him sneaking to the back door to meet Lin Sheng and whispering for a long time. Only then does Sister Zhao skip home.

Before dawn, the dew soaks the ankles. Sister Zhao's mother discovers that her daughter has not gotten up at this time. She scolds a few times but gets no response. She searches in the firewood room and finds only an empty quilt. So, she and her old man search everywhere. They run to Liu Laosan's house, but his son is also gone. The old couple are furious and retreat lightly.

Before noon, the news of Lin Sheng and Sister Zhao's disappearance has spread throughout the village.

A Page from a Diary 224

— Xiaoxue

If you can pay attention to what you encounter every day, you will definitely get many valuable materials of various colors. If you record them well, it will become a very valuable collection of thoughts. So, I feel that articles like diaries are indispensable.

Yesterday, I returned to Zhenru from Shanghai and experienced a memorable event on bus number three. At that time, the bus was very crowded. From Baoshan Road to the Sun Temple, I hardly had a moment to relax. The car was shaking so badly that I was suffocating. When we arrived at the Sun Temple, the car became less crowded because some passengers got off. At this time, there was a villager who had a salted fish in his hand. He carelessly pulled the rope tied to the salted fish, letting it move east and west around the passengers. So, a round of unfavorable comments began...

"You are Chinese, why do you want to eat this kind of fish?" said A.

"Our own fresh fish tastes very good. Why do you want to buy this kind of salted fish?" said B.

"Not eating this kind of fish doesn't mean you can't live well!" said C.

"We Chinese are really too disappointing, so the country has become like this... The officials only know how to squeeze the people, and the businessmen only know how to sell enemy goods. We certainly can't tolerate those who squeeze the people now. As for those who sell enemy goods, as long as we don't buy them, they will suffer..." said D.

In this way, one sentence after another, they made the villager blush with shame. He remained silent and did not say a word. He seemed very ashamed and remorseful.

At this time, I felt very strange. Such nationalistic remarks actually came from the mouths of those petty workers in the clothes of ordinary citizens. Who says China is beyond salvation? The people filled with national consciousness make up the majority of China's 400 million people. If the ruling class could make good use of the people and use the power of the people to deal with the enemy's invasion, wouldn't that be a good way?

When the car arrived at Gujiazhai, the villager holding a foreign fish got off. Everyone in the car turned their heads to look at the villager's back. The car continued to move forward, and the villager's back disappeared along with it.

Young Master 225

— Binghui

At about nine o'clock in the morning, the streetcar is the most crowded. Every day, at this time, I can find many familiar faces in the car. Among them, the most eye-catching are a pot-bellied, round-faced, big-nosed man with a civilized beard and a small hat, and a short man with a pointed head, small eyes, and an old blue serge suit who never wears a tie. One tall and one short, both around forty years old, they look very funny. Every time I meet them, they are always together. They can truly be said to be a naturally funny pair. They are quite talented in public speaking and seem to have very deep and broad life experiences. They often gesticulate wildly and talk loudly about wonderful and strange things that make people laugh until their stomachs hurt.

This time, when the car drove to Tibet Road, there was suddenly a majestic and loud military band and singing on the road. There was a slight stir in the car. The car stopped... People's heads stretched out of the car window, looking with surprised and solemn eyes. The short man grabbed my sleeve and shouted for me to look quickly. By the time I squeezed to the window from the crowd, the car had already started moving. I only saw the backs of a group of people moving towards Nichengqiao to the north. It turned out to be the American young master soldiers, the mortar team. The pot-bellied man grabbed this point and began to make comments...

"The American soldiers are so mighty, their military appearance is so neat! I said that those young students who don't know the times shout every day that they want to fight imperialism. Do you think those Chinese soldiers, who are even worse than beggars, can fight these powerful and majestic foreign soldiers? Haha... What a joke..."

"If there really is a fight," the short man naturally chimed in, "as long as the Chinese soldiers look at the shadows of these foreign soldiers, they will be scared and run away! Listen to the military songs they sing. Hearing them makes the hairs on my head stand on end. They are so solemn and terrifying..."

These words struck my eardrums, and the flames of anger in my heart burned. My blood was boiling! I couldn't wait to punch these shameless, cold-blooded things to death. But I was too cowardly and only put my sweaty fists in my pocket. I never had the courage to wave it in front of this villain's face. Shame!

The ball field has arrived... I walked with a lost soul, dejected and dragging a broken heart, all the way into this dark office.

The center also welcomes young people from all walks of life to come and listen.
