Health Weekly

Published every Sunday (Second Issue) Editor of Health Weekly, No. 4 Hongfu Lane, Bridge Pier, North Henan Road, Shanghai

Infantile Convulsions 227

— Guo Boliang

Acute convulsions belong to heat, chronic convulsions belong to cold. Infants under one year old are the most difficult to care for. If there is no fixed time for breastfeeding, it will lead to inconsistent fullness and hunger, or excessive love and frequent teasing, or excessive warmth. All these things can cause the danger of infantile convulsions. Infants are purely Yang in constitution. Their internal organs are not fully developed, and their Qi and blood are insufficient. Once they are sick, whether from external or internal causes, their body fluids will be damaged.

If they catch wind and evil, their body heat does not subside, and they show symptoms such as crying without tears, a blue face, and a dry nose, the internal body fluids have been damaged. The convulsions will begin with symptoms of high fever and red face, confused consciousness, twitching hands and feet, back arching, staring eyes, clenched teeth, and rising phlegm and shortness of breath. This type of convulsion is called acute convulsion.

If there is no cold or heat, the back suddenly arches, the limbs twitch, the stool appears blue-white, phlegm rises, and the breath is short and the corners of the mouth are crooked, this type of convulsion is called chronic convulsion.

There are also cases where acute and chronic convulsions occur simultaneously. However, it is necessary to observe the number of symptoms of acute and chronic convulsions before determining whether it is a heat or cold syndrome. Generally, acute convulsions belong to heat, and chronic convulsions belong to cold. Acute convulsions are mostly due to liver heat, and chronic convulsions are mostly due to spleen cold. The treatment for acute convulsions should focus on clearing heat, resolving phlegm, extinguishing wind, and generating body fluids. The treatment for chronic convulsions should focus on warming and invigorating the middle, and resolving phlegm. Therefore, when you see a child is sick, do not panic. First, examine whether it is cold or heat, and then consult a doctor for diagnosis and treatment. Do not blindly believe in witchcraft. Unfortunately, parents all over the world, when they see a child suffering from convulsions, are invariably panicked and at a loss. Some seek witchcraft, some seek miraculous prescriptions, and all kinds of methods are mixed up, resulting in the child's death, which is truly sad.

Scrofula of the Neck 228

There is a saying that sores, no matter how big or small, are good when pus comes out. This refers to local surgery. In the case of scrofula, those that have not broken and ulcerated can still be expected to dissipate. Those that have broken and discharged pus and want to heal are rarely seen. It must be known that scrofula is a systemic disease. It cannot be concluded as a local surgical problem simply because there are cervical lymph node tuberculosis without any pain. Those who do not understand medical knowledge often think that it is a minor local problem and do not care about it. They often use European methods to dig it out or use proven prescriptions to apply mercury plasters. Therefore, it is often seen that although scrofula is removed, the internal toxins are not completely eliminated, and it recurs again and again, leading to death. This journal, in order to seek happiness for society, must tell you in detail.

The neck is where the lymph nodes are concentrated. The function of the lymph nodes is to eliminate pathogens. Congenital hereditary tuberculosis and syphilis are contained in the whole body due to bloodline relationships. Scrofula occurs when the lymph nodes lose their ability to kill bacteria and instead become tuberculous and swollen. The "Su Wen" calls scrofula "mouse fistula." Later generations of prescription books believed that scrofula was caused by accidentally eating food gnawed by rats, which is actually speculation. The "Su Wen" refers to broken and ulcerated ones as "mouse fistula." The "Ling Shu" says that those that have ulcerated are fistulas, and those that have not ulcerated are scrofula. This disease is more common in young and strong people and less common in the elderly. Examining the cause, it is generally nothing more than the poison inherited from parents.

In the early stage of scrofula, the nodules are the size of beans or like peach pits or chestnuts, in clusters of four or five, and often connected to the root of the ear and to the supraclavicular fossa, or from left to right, or from right to left. Mild scrofula can be pinched and pushed up and down, left and right, and moved freely. Over time, they gradually enlarge and cannot be pushed. After half a year or a year or two, they will break and discharge pus. Before breaking, they must be soft and the color does not change, or there may be slight pain, but it is often painless. Those due to congenital tuberculosis have thin and clear pus that flows continuously. Those due to hereditary syphilis have turbid and thick pus and have an odor.

The above is true scrofula. There is also a kind of pseudo-scrofula. For example, throat disease, cough, childhood smallpox, measles. Although the underlying disease is cured, the nodules in the neck and under the jaw often resemble scrofula and do not dissipate for a long time. Do not mistake them for scrofula. After the illness, the healthy Qi has not recovered and the toxins have not been exhausted. When the body becomes stronger, it can dissipate on its own. Those that are delayed for a long time must also consult a doctor for diagnosis and treatment to avoid inducing other diseases.

Some cases of scrofula are easy to cure, some are difficult to cure, and some are ineffective even with treatment. These questions are of the greatest concern to patients. It is not difficult to solve this problem. Just understand its truth.

Common Knowledge of Blood Disorders - A Discussion of Blood Disorders (II) 229

— Ding Jihua

Causes of Vomiting Blood

The blood in the human body circulates through the vessels, flowing up and down in a continuous cycle. Outwardly, it reaches the skin, and inwardly, it connects to the internal organs. In a healthy person, the circulation is unobstructed. Conversely, there will be illness. But what blood relies on is the vessels, and what the vessels rely on is Qi. Blood flows through the vessels because of Qi, and the vessels are strengthened because of Qi. This blood circulation can follow Qi to flow and not lose its normal course. If a vessel is stimulated, the blood in the vessel will inevitably rupture and overflow. If Qi can fully maintain the blood vessels, then the blood in the vessel will naturally not overflow. Otherwise, if Qi is deficient and cannot maintain the blood vessels, the blood in the vessel may overflow on its own even without stimulation. Examining the causes of blood overflowing outside the vessels due to stimulation, one is due to stimulation, and the other is due to Qi not being able to maintain the blood vessels. The former belongs to the real syndrome, and the latter belongs to the false syndrome. Although they are both vomiting blood, the symptoms are very different. In short, vomiting blood due to stimulation is due to fire forcing the blood to rise, and vomiting blood due to Qi deficiency is due to insufficient Qi that cannot control the blood.

Vomiting Blood Due to Stimulation

Vomiting blood due to stimulation includes injury to the liver after great anger, which is commonly referred to as anger injuring the liver. After great anger, the liver immediately expands, and liver fire follows. The liver is the place where blood is stored. Once liver fire is strong, the fire will boil the blood vessels. The liver governs Qi, and if Qi rises, it cannot control the blood. The blood rises with the Qi, and the blood vessels are broken by the fire and overflow. This is one type of vomiting blood due to stimulation. There is also vomiting blood due to a harsh environment. People in harsh environments must have more thoughts, worries, and sorrows than ordinary people, and they are depressed and unhappy all day long. Examining the source of the disease, it is also due to the liver. All the emotional disturbances in life are managed by the liver. Therefore, those with emotional depression are more likely to suffer from this disease. There are also those who vomit blood after being greatly shocked. After the shock, the blood boils, and the transport of Qi and blood vessels remains the same, blocked and stagnant, causing the blood vessels to tighten or run horizontally and reversely, resulting in vomiting blood that cannot be stopped. The situation is extremely dangerous when the symptoms occur, with the appearance of not being able to live to the next day. However, if the vomiting due to shock is not related to the heart meridian, it is easier to treat than vomiting due to shock related to the emotions. Being unrelated to the heart meridian means that the shock is sudden, and although there is temporary shock, there is not much pain or itching in the heart meridian after the matter is over. This type of vomiting blood is easier to treat. Vomiting blood due to shock related to the emotions refers to the shock that comes as something that should happen in psychological fantasy and panic, and is suddenly related to one's own personal interests. After the matter is over, one cannot calmly forget it. This type of vomiting blood is more difficult to treat, because if the shock is too severe and the network vessels rupture, and emotions are depressed afterwards, Qi is injured again. When Qi rises, the blood will overflow from the broken blood vessels from time to time, so it is difficult to treat. (To be continued)

Medical Advice 230

— Answered by Ding Jihua

Dry Cough

Mr. Du Haoen wrote to me saying that I returned from a social engagement at the end of last month. Suddenly, I had a cough and my throat was very dry. After coughing for a long time, I finally had a small amount of phlegm, which was very dark in color. The illness is not serious, but my uncle has had lung disease for two years. Is it contagious pulmonary tuberculosis or just a common cough? I would like to get a proper treatment to relieve my worries.

Answer: Coughing up phlegm that is not smooth and always feeling dry in the throat is called a dry cough. The lung is a delicate organ that is responsible for clearing and cleaning. Dryness attacks the lung, and the lung fluid does not moisten the stagnated heat, which remains in the lung network, resulting in unfavorable breathing and coughing due to Qi rising in reverse. This symptom is caused by dry weather and is not pulmonary tuberculosis. There is no need to worry, but patients often do not pay much attention when the cough first starts. One must know that even if the initial cough is not tuberculosis, it is always due to lung disease. A lung cough that does not heal can lead to tuberculosis over time. Therefore, although a dry cough is a minor illness, one must be careful. I have attached a prescription below. Take it warm in the evening. All tobacco, alcohol, and other items must also be avoided.

Two mace of frost leaves, two mace of peeled apricot kernels, eight fen of cicada slough, one and a half mace of snakegourd peel, two mace of fritillary bulb, two mace of large ophiopogon root, three loquat leaves.

Malaria Mother - Mr. Yu Jiayun wrote to me saying that my mother is over sixty years old and has a history of coughing and vomiting blood. It recurs from time to time. It has been going on for two or three years. In August of this year, it recurred several times, vomiting blood. A month later, she had chills and fever again, which caused her to be bedridden. The chills and fever came like malaria. The fever was so severe that she was unconscious. After lying in bed for more than a month, the chills and fever stopped. Suddenly, she had abdominal pain that was unbearable. After two or three days, her abdomen gradually became enlarged and the pain stopped. However, her abdomen was distended like a drum, which was worse after eating. There was also a mass inside. The condition changed several times, and treatment was difficult. I dare to ask for a treatment. I would be very grateful.

Answer: Your mother's abdominal distension is due to malaria. This is a malaria mother and not drum distension. The cause of malaria is the feeling of seasonal evil that obstructs phlegm and stagnation. After malaria, the phlegm stagnation does not resolve, and the liver and spleen Qi mechanism is not harmonious. There is often abdominal pain and distension. Your mother has a history of coughing and vomiting blood. Qi and Yin deficiency makes adjustment and treatment difficult. Now I plan to use the Guangji Ao Jia Decoction to treat it. Maybe it can turn danger into safety.

Eight fen of stir-fried tortoise shell, eight fen of peony root, eight fen of immature orange, three mace of codonopsis, five fen of chebulae peel, five fen of raw rhubarb, four fen of tangerine peel, two fen of cassia bark.

Grind the right medicine into honey pills the size of a parasol tree seed. Take twenty pills daily with boiled water, or decoct and take it.

Common Knowledge

Cold 231

The weather in winter is cold and easy to catch a cold. In severe cases, the nose is blocked, there is a lot of phlegm, and the voice is not clear, which easily causes early lung disease. For treatment, decoct three mace of ephedra with water and smell it between the nostrils. It can heal on its own.

囗Low Back Pain 232

The waist bones often feel sore and painful, especially in women and the elderly. This symptom is mostly due to deficiency of both the liver and kidneys, and damp heat remains in the network channels. Long-term consumption of black fungus and teasel meat can cure it.

囗Red Streak Phlebitis 233

This symptom is particularly dangerous. If it grows on the toes or back of the foot, and the red streaks reach the navel, it is incurable. If it grows on the fingers or back of the hand, and the red streaks reach the heart and chest, it is incurable. If it grows on the lips, and the red streaks reach the throat, it is incurable. There is a saying that "looking at phlebitis on a galloping horse" refers to red streak phlebitis. Anyone suffering from red streak phlebitis, whether on the hand or foot, can apply red plaster to dissolve it. This plaster is sold in all major pharmacies.
